Current Commentary

Japan's New Diplomatic Strategy Towards China 36

Since the signing of the North China Ceasefire Agreement, the impossibility of recovering lost territories by force has been generally acknowledged by the Chinese people. Henceforth, the outcome of the struggle between China and Japan over the issue of the Eastern Provinces must be decided on the international diplomatic arena. Japan, taking advantage of this opportunity, has recently deployed a new diplomatic strategy towards China, the outlines of which are already visible to us. 1) Appointing Ishii Kikujiro as the Japanese representative to the World Economic Conference, while simultaneously tasking him with the mission of explaining Japan's policies and discrediting China's reputation on the international stage. This is because after Matsuoka Yosuke's brash and reckless tactics failed and Kajiwara returned to Japan, the Japanese authorities, in an attempt to struggle again and strive for victory later, have deployed this auxiliary force as a means of preparing for future developments. 2) Hoping to shift world opinion, and preparing to engage in sophistry by discussing the "Manchukuo" issue at the Pacific Conference in late August, in order to explain Japan's so-called position. For this purpose, they have dispatched eloquent individuals from within the country, such as Nitobe Inazo and Tsurumi Yusuke, to Canada. 3) The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs is creating an atmosphere for changing diplomatic policy towards China, propagating "abandoning the policy of neither attachment nor detachment towards China, and adopting a proactive policy of friendly relations with China." The dissemination of this kind of atmosphere is intended on the one hand to lure the Chinese authorities into their trap, and on the other hand to persuade the international diplomatic community to advise China to recognize the enemy as a friend, thereby undermining China's hard-won position in the League of Nations. The aforementioned new diplomatic strategy of Japan towards China involves a three-pronged offensive, meticulously planned. The first and second lines of attack are deployed because they are clearly aware that although the League of Nations General Assembly has passed a report unfavorable to Japan, and the Advisory Committee has resolved on measures to not recognize the puppet organization, for the time being there are no more active and effective means to impose sanctions on the aggressor. Now, at a time when military action has achieved considerable objectives, they are exerting all their efforts to attack China's position in the international diplomatic arena, and to rebuild Japan's diplomatic front. Their intention is that even if they cannot immediately turn defeat into victory, they can use this to ease the situation, so that China's progress cannot be accelerated, in order to gradually reap the benefits of the third line of attack or even deploy a fourth line of attack. As the facts show, today's Sino-Japanese struggle on the international diplomatic stage has passed the stage of fierce assaults and is now a prolonged trench warfare. If we cannot break through the diplomatic front deployed by Japan today, then China's future failure in international diplomacy will likely be even more embarrassing than the events of Miyun and Tanggu.

Ishii's speech in the United States is in fact the first activity after Japan deployed its new diplomatic strategy towards China. He attacked economic resistance and demanded that the Non-War Pact be considered illegal, so that countries would no longer use this method as a tool of national policy, and falsely claimed that "For the past twenty years, China has been constantly attacking Japan economically, and Japan has been its victim." This is still the old argument that Matsuoka refuted at the League of Nations conference last winter. However, Ishii's speech this time is only a first attempt. We cannot ignore it simply because it reiterates Matsuoka's old argument. Japan's new diplomatic strategy towards China is now gradually unfolding. Will our countrymen concentrate their efforts to deal with it?

The World Economic Conference is About to Open

The Venue is Decorated Splendidly 37

The British Monarch Prepares to Attend and Deliver a Speech

Welcoming Representatives from All Countries

(London) Hundreds of people are currently busy day and night at the new Royal Geological Museum in South Kensington, preparing everything so that the British Monarch can welcome representatives from 66 countries participating in the World Economic Conference there on Monday. The main hall, which previously housed geological specimens, is now being heavily decorated, making it exceptionally magnificent, so that it can accommodate an unprecedented international gathering of politicians and experts in London. At one end of the hall, a giant altar in dark green, gold, and three colors has been set up. The British Monarch will deliver a speech through a loudspeaker on top, which will be broadcast around the world. There are also 24 other loudspeakers that will transmit the speech to the 20-odd listeners nearby. A high platform has been set up on the side of the hall to accommodate film and recording equipment. After the brief opening ceremony, the British Monarch will leave the venue, and Chairman MacDonald will deliver a speech. For the first few days of the conference, the chief representatives of various countries will speak on the causes of the global economic downturn and how to remedy it. A total of 2,000 participants will enjoy various special privileges, such as exemptions from licensing restrictions, and unprecedented large-scale facilities for telephone, telegraph, and transportation to all parts of the world. The conference will provide famous wines from around the world to quench the thirst of the representatives during discussions. A 70-foot-long wine room has been built under the venue, so that representatives can choose their favorite beverages to relax and enjoy the pleasure of being at home. The wines provided have been purchased by the conference's beverage provider after consulting with the consulates of various countries stationed in London in advance. It can be said that it is a collection of famous wines from all over the world. (Eighth day Reuters)

Our Delegation is Busy 38

Preparing a Document to Declare its Aims

(London) Chinese Finance Minister Song Ziwen and the entire Chinese delegation held a long meeting today to prepare for the World Economic Conference. Minister Song has not yet arranged a meeting with British officials, but is quite busy and has drafted a document declaring China's aims, which is expected to be released soon. Currently, its content is not to be disclosed in advance. (Eighth day Reuters)

(London) Reuters has learned that Song Ziwen, the chief representative of China attending the World Economic Conference, does not wish to issue any declaration on the Far East or economic issues at this time. The China Committee of the House of Commons will host a banquet to entertain Mr. Song next Tuesday. (Seventh day Reuters)

US Delegation Arrives in British Territory 39

Plymouth, the US delegation to the Economic Conference arrived here today. When Secretary of State Hull met with reporters, he emphasized that the United States hopes that the Economic Conference can greatly reduce international trade barriers, ultimately leading to the revival of international trade, and declared that they would not discuss the war debt issue, as this matter is completely outside the scope of the Economic Conference, nor would they discuss the issue of disarmament, as this matter will be entirely under the authority of Davis and Washington. (Eighth day National Telegram)

Preliminary Talks between Britain, the US, and France 40

(London) According to responsible sources, the preliminary talks of the Economic Conference will be held tomorrow evening by representatives of the finance ministries and central banks of Britain, France, and the United States. The focus will be on international monetary issues, such as the disturbances caused by currency devaluation, and on the remedies proposed by various countries. These talks will continue until Sunday afternoon. (Eighth day Havas Telegram)

(Washington) It was learned today from reliable sources that the United States will propose at the World Economic Conference the adoption of an international fictitious gold unit, to which the currencies of all countries in the world will be fixed at a definite ratio. This unit will be defined as a standard for international currency values based on a certain fineness and weight of gold, but it will not be used as a commonly used international currency. The US President and his advisors believe that this is the most practical and feasible way to stabilize exchange rates and can avoid speculative behavior on various currencies around the world. Therefore, the value of this fictitious gold unit will not be allowed to fluctuate. As for its weight in gold, it will be approximately between the pure gold content of the gold franc and the US dollar. The United States does not insist on this. If all countries can agree to this plan, it intends to first stipulate the ratio of the gold dollar and the gold pound to this fictitious gold unit, and then move on to the currencies of other countries. (Seventh day National Telegram)

Germany Demands Trade Outlets 41

(Berlin) Germany will demand at the Economic Conference the removal of tariff barriers and the provision of convenience for German exports. Its main reason is that if foreign countries, especially creditor countries, do not provide Germany with export facilities, its ability to repay foreign debt will be severely hit. Although the total amount of Germany's foreign trade has been reduced to one-third during the economic downturn, it has still been able to maintain a huge trade surplus. For example, in 1931, the trade surplus was 2.87 billion marks, and in 1932, the trade surplus was 1.07 billion marks, so it was able to repay all foreign debts and even repay part of the principal. However, in the first three months of this year, there was only a trade surplus of more than 112.7 million marks. According to this situation, it is clearly insufficient to repay foreign debt interest. However, the import of food and industrial raw materials has been reduced to the point where it cannot be reduced any further. There is no way to increase the trade surplus other than promoting exports. (Eighth day National Telegram)

Roosevelt Expresses His Views on the War Debt Issue 42

Saying He is Willing to Receive Any Application from Debtor Nations

Enjoying the Privilege of Relief Under the Constitution

(New York) President Roosevelt issued a new statement today, expressing his willingness to receive any formal requests regarding the modification of war debts, and declaring that the first step must be initiated by the debtor nations. According to US presidential advisors, regardless of Congress's attitude towards the deferral of war debts, President Roosevelt enjoys the power to grant relief under the Constitution. (Eighth day Reuters)

(Washington) President Roosevelt informed congressional leaders that in order for Congress to adjourn this week, he did not wish to ask Congress to grant him the power to negotiate tariff agreements. (Seventh day Reuters)

(Washington) The British government will not pay the war debt owed to the United States that is due on June 15. There is no comment from London. According to non-official opinions here, Britain will inevitably default, forcing the United States to decide on its position on this issue. Officials still believe that since President Roosevelt has not yet received a formal application from the debtor country regarding this issue, the payment due on June 15 will definitely be paid in full. The French Ambassador to the United States, Lai Bo Lai, visited the White House today to meet with President Roosevelt. It is claimed that the purpose of Lai's visit to President Roosevelt was to ascertain the attitude of the United States, rather than to make a specific request. Judging from the situation, any attempt to stabilize currencies before internal price relations have been ascertained is too premature. Britain and the United States have already agreed on this point. (Seventh day Reuters)

Britain Rejects Japanese Goods, the Japanese Government Plans to Retaliate 43

Formally Protesting Against Increased Taxes on India

(Tokyo) According to what appears to be reliable sources, the Japanese government is currently considering increasing import taxes on British goods in order to retaliate against Britain and India's plans to reject Japanese trade. (Eighth day Reuters)

(Tokyo) According to a telegram received by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, in order to promote trade, the British government has recently notified the League of Nations Secretariat that it has decided to withdraw from the Treaty on the Abolition of Import and Export Prohibitions and Restrictions established by the Economic Committee of the League of Nations in July 1928. This means that Britain has completely abandoned its traditional free trade policy and is expelling Japanese goods from India and British colonies. The Japanese government has no choice but to seek retaliatory measures and is currently studying countermeasures. (Eighth day Dentsu Telegram)

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Uchida telegraphed Director General Miyake of Calcutta last night regarding the protest to the Indian government against the new tariffs, stating in essence that although this measure by your government does not violate the treaty, it is inappropriate to take this action before the meeting of the British Conference. There is much heated debate in our country, casting a shadow on the future of relations between the two countries. Therefore, the Imperial Government, in light of this, sincerely hopes that your government will give it consideration. (Eighth day Dentsu Telegram)

(Tokyo) According to a telegram from Consul General Nishimura in India today, although Indian tariffs have been increased, the Indian government has unofficially expressed its readiness to negotiate with Japan in order to resolve trade difficulties. It is reported that before receiving the above-mentioned news, the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs had telegraphed the Japanese Consul General to formally negotiate with the Indian government regarding the tax increase. Officials stated today that if the Indian government can give adequate consideration to Japan's position, Japan is prepared to find ways to manage exports or propose the price of exports. Otherwise, Japan will inevitably consider retaliatory measures. (Eighth day Reuters)

Pacific Coast

Radio Broadcasting War 44

Russia and the US Plan to Establish Large Radio Networks

Japan, Being Surrounded, Feels Extremely Embarrassed

(Tokyo) A radio supremacy war is occurring on the Pacific coast. Japanese radio broadcasting is sometimes obstructed by the radio waves of the 75-kilowatt radio station in Nanjing. The Ministry of Communications is currently planning to establish a 100-kilowatt radio station in Fukuoka to counter Nanjing. However, this plan is not easy to implement due to the impact on other radio stations in Japan. Just as the Ministry of Communications is struggling with this, there is news that makes the Ministry of Communications embarrassed: in the Soviet Union's second five-year plan, it is attempting to complete the radio network in northeastern Siberia, planning to establish 50-kilowatt radio stations in Vladivostok, Nikolayevsk, Khabarovsk, Omsk, Tomsk, and other places to develop resources and popularize education. The Soviet Union's broadcasting of Communist ideology has made the Japanese authorities nervous. After the Soviet Union's plan is realized this time, difficult problems will inevitably arise. The US authorities, stimulated by the Soviet Union's plan, are attempting to establish a large radio network on the west coast. How Japan will establish a plan in the Pacific radio wave supremacy war is a very interesting question. (Eighth day Japanese United Press Telegram)

Korean Woman Plots to Assassinate Muto 45

Vowing to Avenge Her Husband

Unexpectedly, the Plot Was Leaked and She Was Arrested

(Harbin) A 61-year-old Korean woman, who plotted to assassinate the Commander of the Kwantung Army, Muto, was arrested in advance, which prevented the plan from being carried out. The ban on newspapers reporting on this was lifted after the investigation came to an end. The woman's name is Nam Ja-hyeon. Twenty years ago, her husband was beaten by the Japanese, so she extremely hated the Japanese and repeatedly plotted revenge. Since then, she has been engaged in the Korean independence movement, traveling between Manchuria and Korea. In April of the second year of Showa, she plotted to assassinate Governor-General Saito in Seoul, but failed. She sneaked into Manchuria, based in Harbin, and plotted to assassinate Commander Muto, carrying bombs and a pistol, intending to carry out the plan in Changchun on National Foundation Day on March 1. She was arrested by consulate police on February 20 when she departed from Harbin. (Eighth day Dentsu Telegram)

A Great Step Forward After the Locarno Treaty

Signing of the Four-Power Pact 49

"A United Front to Guarantee Peace in All of Europe

Not a United Front Against Any Country"

Mussolini's Proud Achievement

After formally signing the initial letters of the Four-Power Peace Pact with representatives from Britain, France, and Germany at 7:30 PM tonight, the Prime Minister of Rome, Mussolini, immediately outlined the text of the agreement to the lower house of Parliament, declaring that this agreement guarantees peace throughout Europe. He also said that the purpose of this agreement is not aimed specifically at any one country, but to obligate the signatory countries to strive to make disarmament effective. He also claimed that this agreement is not a united front against any country, but a united front to maintain peace. If the complete restoration of the economy and the maintenance of peace are to be sought, cooperation with the United States is indispensable. Furthermore, France has now joined us and no longer follows a policy of isolation, which is sufficient to guarantee peace in Europe. Mussolini then traced the peace agreements since the European War, calling the Locarno Pact the first milestone on the path to complete understanding, and said that the maintenance of normal relations between the signatory countries of this agreement is essential to the maintenance of normalcy by all countries. This agreement already contains all the principles of the League of Nations Covenant, which is sufficient to guarantee peace for all countries, etc. (Seventh day National Telegram)

Rome heard that Germany had not yet made a firm expression of acceptance of the Four-Power Pact yesterday morning. In the afternoon, Mussolini personally spoke with German Chancellor Hitler by telephone. It was then that Germany agreed to sign the agreement. (Eighth day Reuters)

Full Text of the Four-Power Peace Pact 50

Preamble

The governments of the four countries, knowing their responsibilities as permanent members of the International League of Nations' administrative council and as signatories to the Locarno Treaty, and firmly believing that the world's restless atmosphere cannot be eliminated unless they consolidate their mutual responsibilities, are willing to faithfully fulfill the Locarno Treaty, the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and the Declaration on the Prohibition of the Use of Violence, and are willing to make the League of Nations Covenant fully effective in accordance with the predetermined procedures without violating it, and to respect the rights of all countries, therefore, agree on the following articles:

1. The contracting countries shall consult with each other on issues related to themselves and agree to strive for effective cooperation by all countries within the scope of the International League of Nations to maintain peace.

2. The contracting countries shall agree to study together any suggestions made regarding various methods and procedures for making the provisions of this agreement as effective as possible, especially regarding Articles 10, 16, and 19 of the Covenant. However, the power to make decisions shall still be exercised by the competent authorities of the International League of Nations. (Note: Article 10 of the International League of Nations Covenant respects and maintains the territorial integrity of member states of the League of Nations, Article 16 is the sanction against those who violate the agreement, and Article 19 is the amendment of the treaty.)

3. The contracting countries shall do their best to make the Disarmament Conference a success, and agree that after the Disarmament Conference is closed, if there are still issues that are particularly relevant to the contracting countries that remain unresolved, the contracting countries shall re-examine them with each other.

4. The contracting countries shall consult with each other on all economic issues related to their respective interests within the scope of the International League of Nations, especially the economic recovery of Europe.

5. The effective period of this agreement is set at ten years. If there is no notice of termination after eight years of implementation, it shall be extended indefinitely and continue to be effective. However, each contracting country may still give advance notice of termination two years in advance.

6. This agreement shall be written in the languages of the four countries. In case of doubt, the French language shall prevail. Each contracting country shall ratify it as soon as possible. The documents of ratification shall be kept by the Italian government, which shall issue a certificate to each contracting country, certifying that the documents of ratification have been delivered. This agreement shall take effect from the date on which the documents of ratification of all contracting countries have been delivered, and shall be submitted to the International League of Nations for registration in accordance with the provisions of the International League of Nations Covenant.

The Four-Power Signing Opens

A New Historical Era 51

The People of Rome Cheered Loudly

Rome, the Four-Power Pact, which aims to guarantee peace in Europe, was finally signed here tonight at the Palazzo Venezia by representatives of Britain, France, Germany, and Italy after weeks of exhaustive and sometimes seemingly hopeless negotiations. After the German government's telegram approving the agreement was transmitted from Berlin, the ceremony was held at 7:30 PM. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini addressed the Senate, whose audience was packed with diplomatic personnel, stating that although this agreement has been amended, it does not change the spirit of the original draft. This agreement is not made against one or several countries, nor does it establish a united front. The difficulties that have been overcome are mostly concentrated in Article 3 of the agreement, which stipulates that if the Disarmament Conference fails, the four powers should consult with each other to seek methods to resolve outstanding issues. Now that this agreement has been ratified, it can achieve ten years of peace. The four countries, in accordance with the adopted plan, reiterate their hope that the Disarmament Conference will be successful. This agreement does not mean that its will is imposed on other countries in the form of hegemony or rule. Britain had foreseen the possibility of this agreement from the beginning. Italy and Britain, with their balanced position in Europe, have achieved a special duty based on the Locarno Pact. Its new expression and its possibilities can be seen in the Four-Power Pact. France has never opposed this agreement. France has shown a model of cooperation for agreements that must be realized. All special issues that separate France and Italy from Germany and France can be resolved within the atmosphere of this agreement through bilateral agreements that do not go beyond the scope and spirit of this agreement. The full text of this agreement has now been published and is slightly different from the semi-official news transmitted from Paris yesterday. This agreement will be implemented after it is formally signed in Rome. The signing ceremony was quite simple. The Italian Prime Minister represented Italy in signing the agreement, and the British, French, and German ambassadors also signed the first word in succession. When this agreement was signed, crowds gathered outside the Palazzo Venezia, cheering endlessly, deafeningly, knowing that this agreement would create a new history. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, at the ardent request of the crowd, appeared on the balcony. After the cheering subsided, he briefly addressed the crowd. The Italians view the conclusion of this agreement as one of Mussolini's greatest achievements, which can consolidate his position as a world statesman and have the potential to influence the future of Europe. (Seventh day Reuters)

Italy is Overjoyed

People Formed Processions to Celebrate 52

Rome, after Prime Minister Mussolini's speech in the Senate regarding the Four-Power Pact, all members of parliament and attendees stood up, requesting that the speech be widely publicized. Senate President Federzoni immediately ordered it to be done. Throughout Italy, upon hearing of the establishment of the Four-Power Pact, people rejoiced with singing and dancing. The Prime Minister's speech was broadcast everywhere via radio and made into gramophone records. In Florence and Bari, people formed processions to celebrate. Newspapers all published extra editions. The "Tribune" reported that the Four-Power Pact is Prime Minister Mussolini's current undertaking to control European and global political situations.

Rome, the establishment of the Four-Power Pact and Prime Minister Mussolini's speech evoked enthusiastic responses in various Italian cities. In Milan, Turin, Genoa, Verona, Brescia, Livorno, Salerno, Cesena, Trapani and other cities, crowds listened to the Prime Minister's speech broadcast by speakers, cheering Mussolini's name and marching in processions. Provincial governors gave speeches to the people. Workers in Naples decided to hold a grand demonstration on Saturday and Sunday. Newspapers paid much attention to Paris' attitude. Reviews in French newspapers that mentioned the possibility of a French-Italian compromise were recorded in detail. "Le Matin" stated that the long-term improvement of French-Italian relations would finally dispel France's suspicions about the Four-Power Pact. Prime Minister Daladier's speech on the possibility of concluding a French-Italian pact was reprinted by various newspapers. "Il Tevere" reported that Mussolini's ideal is to have the major powers that bear the greatest responsibility in Europe provide long-term guarantees of peace. This ideal has made great progress and is in line with the sentiments of the people, which are more powerful than the usual diplomatic techniques. Europe today is tired of cunning tricks and yearns for life. "Le Matin" said that the Four-Power Pact marks the beginning of a new era in history, a vast picture representing revival, progress, and prosperity, unfolding a bright path. This is what Mussolini's speech indicated to the world. Human civilization found a savior in Rome yesterday. (Havas, 8th)

France Feels Pleased

And Will Improve French-Italian Relations 53

(Paris) The news that the representatives of Britain, France, and Germany initialed the Four-Power Pact with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini in Rome was received here with great satisfaction because French officials deeply feared that further delays would affect Berlin's attitude. Officials in the French government believe that the signing of this pact is the first stage in easing the European situation. With this pact established, negotiations will soon continue to determine the practical scope of the Four-Power Pact and to improve relations between France and Italy, and further to seek improvement in relations between Italy and the Little Entente countries. France has been planning this diplomatic procedure for several years. Its significance lies in striving to expand the possibility of coordination among all countries without sacrificing existing treaties. French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour has verbally assured the Little Entente countries of this intention. The French authorities are prepared to make another statement, assuring that all countries close to France will receive the same reassurance. Prime Minister Daladier and Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour will explain the contents of the Four-Power Pact to the Chamber of Deputies on Friday. (Havas, 7th)

Rome, after French Ambassador to Italy Jouvenel had a lengthy telephone conversation with French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour yesterday, he will now visit Italian Prime Minister Mussolini to convey that the French government was greatly moved by Mussolini's speech in the Senate yesterday, which mentioned the possibility of resolving outstanding issues between France and Italy. There are many issues awaiting resolution between France and Italy, but there is hope that talks on current issues, especially disarmament, will proceed smoothly. (Havas, 8th)

Rome, after the Four-Power Pact was agreed upon, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has pardoned Professor Édouard, a Frenchman who was convicted in February for espionage in Italy and sentenced to five years in prison. The trial of this professor, who is the principal of a famous military academy in Paris, had caused much concern between France and Italy. It is reported today that the professor will stay in Italy for a few days to recuperate. (Reuters, 8th)

Germany Reluctantly Agrees

Expressing a Policy of Forced Restraint 54

(Berlin) The official German position is that the Four-Power Pact, in its current diluted form, has not realized its hopes, but that in the current era, the fact that an agreement could be reached at all is very important. This pact is a new starting point for handling difficult European political issues. Much importance is attached to the clause regarding the revision of the peace treaty, but it is regrettable that the pact fails to reconcile the French and German views on equality in armaments. The Germans clearly stated that they could not accept the French demand for the right to supervise German armaments, and also stated that Germany's declaration of December 5 regarding equality in armaments and Chancellor Hitler's statements in the Reichstag last month remain valid and are not restricted by the Four-Power Pact. (Reuters, 8th)

(Berlin) This morning, commentaries on the signing of the Four-Power Pact occupy an important place in the newspapers. Some newspapers, while acknowledging the importance of the pact, expressed reservations about the points that were revised from the first draft, wanting to place the blame on France. The "Völkischer Beobachter" praised the treaty the most, stating, "The Four-Power Pact is the most important treaty in fifteen years. Europe should be grateful to Mussolini and Hitler, as this is their new willingness to maintain European peace with the most resolute attitude." The "Tägliche Rundschau" stated that the German government's sincerity in advocating equality is already very evident, and therefore has the right to hope that the disarmament conference can achieve tangible results, in other words, actual disarmament. As of today, no country has any reason to evade the obligation of actual disarmament. "Kreuzzeitung" said that foreign countries have made various accusations against Germany. Now that the German authorities have shown forced restraint and recognized the Four-Power Pact, the foreign rumors against Germany can be stopped. (Havas, 7th)

(Berlin) According to well-informed sources in political circles, although Foreign Minister Neurath and several other parties continue to oppose the Four-Power Pact, Chancellor Hitler personally attaches great importance to the conclusion of this pact. Therefore, in the end, Germany decided to withdraw its amendments and resolutely sign the final draft agreed upon by the various countries. (Havas, 7th)

Britain Makes No Reservations 55

(London) British officials said that the rumor that Britain's acceptance of the Four-Power Pact was conditional on Germany's joining is completely untrue. Britain supports the draft of the Four-Power Pact and has not raised this reservation. (Havas, 7th)

(Geneva) The initialing and publication of the Four-Power Pact are considered a welcome event here and a sign of the easing of the international situation. The interests of countries other than the four powers and the interests of the League of Nations are all protected, which is very good. Disarmament Again Reaches a Critical Juncture

US, British, and French Paris Conference Opens 58

British and American Representatives Exert Great Pressure on France

The Fate of the London Conference Depends on This Move

(Geneva) Various major points of contention, such as security, naval and air disarmament, and the definition of aggressor nations, have once again plunged the disarmament conference into a state of decline. For this reason, the General Committee has decided to adjourn the meeting until June 27. Chairman Henderson will travel to London at the end of this week to consult with the delegations of various countries gathered there to attend the World Economic Conference, in order to eliminate various obstacles that prevent the conclusion of a convention. The hopes of the general public are now focused on the talks among the representatives of Britain, France, and the United States to be held at the French Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Paris tomorrow. (Reuters, 7th)

(Paris) The American representative Davis has arrived here, preparing to hold disarmament talks at the French Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 8th. Britain will be represented by Foreign Secretary Eden and Air Minister Londonderry. The purpose of this meeting is to achieve some progress on the disarmament issue before the opening of the World Economic Conference on the 1st of next month. In short, Davis hopes to persuade French Prime Minister Daladier to accept the following equation: "Management equals security, which equals disarmament." However, according to the opinions of general observers, it is not easy to persuade France to sacrifice heavy artillery and tanks in exchange for the management it fears lacks substance. According to a Reuters correspondent in Berlin, Berlin regards tomorrow's talks at the French Ministry of Foreign Affairs as the last resort to save the disarmament talks from failure. Political circles in Berlin now believe that British and American representatives intend to exert significant pressure on French cabinet members to reveal what concessions France is prepared to make. If this move is unsuccessful, the disarmament talks will inevitably be unable to continue. All circles in Germany now believe that if disarmament falls into this stalemate, it will be nothing less than the prelude to the failure of the World Economic Conference. (Reuters, 7th)

(Paris) Talks among the representatives of Britain, France, and the United States on the disarmament issue were held at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at 10:40 this morning. French Prime Minister Daladier participated in the talks. Those attending from the British side were Air Minister Londonderry, Foreign Secretary Eden, Counselor of the Embassy in France Campbell, and the head of the League of Nations Section of the Foreign Office Cadogan. Those attending from the American side were Chief Disarmament Representative Davis, Legal Advisor Dulles, and Colonel Strohm, a member of the American Disarmament Delegation. (Havas, 8th)

Decided to Use the British Draft As

The Basis for a Disarmament Convention 59

French Representatives Vigorously Oppose

(Geneva) Today, the General Committee on Disarmament, disregarding fierce French opposition, decided to accept the British draft as the basis for a disarmament convention. Before the vote, the French representatives tried their best to oppose it. The Japanese representatives also stated that Japan cannot accept the provisions prohibiting aerial bombardment unless all aircraft carriers are abolished.

(Guomin News Agency, 8th)

(Geneva) The General Committee on Disarmament decided tonight to adjourn the disarmament conference until June 27. During this period, Chairman Henderson is authorized to continue negotiations in Paris and London, and to convene a special meeting in London if deemed necessary. There are still many unresolved issues within the General Committee. It is reported that US Ambassador Davis will persuade British Prime Minister MacDonald, French Prime Minister Daladier, German Chancellor Hitler, and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini to meet in person as soon as possible, hoping to eliminate the current disagreements. The main points of contention are the issues concerning land, sea, and air defense forces. The provisions on limiting military spending will be completed in the first reading on Thursday, and it is expected that the meeting will be adjourned immediately at that time. Chairman Henderson will revise the British draft during the adjournment, listing several amendments passed by the General Committee in the first reading. It is now believed that it will be possible to decide at the meeting to use the British draft as the basis for the disarmament convention. (Guomin News Agency, 7th)

(Geneva) The French delegation's note to the disarmament conference details France's attitude toward naval armaments. Its principles are as follows: 1. The naval convention should be universal. 2. The principle of mutual interdependence of various armaments should be respected. 3. The actual situation existing at the beginning of the disarmament conference should be taken into account, and the relative proportions of the fleets of various countries should be maintained. However, small naval powers may, in accordance with Article 8 of the League of Nations Covenant, engage in development in appropriate proportions. The provisions of existing naval treaties shall be implemented until December 31, 1936, but the disarmament convention may be subject to strict restrictions. 4. The period of restriction of any armaments in the disarmament convention shall be the same, with sufficient time for various countries to complete their naval construction procedures permitted by the convention during this period. (Havas, 8th)

(Geneva) The Japanese representative to the disarmament conference, Sato, issued a declaration to the General Committee of the conference on behalf of the Japanese government, specifically raising reservations regarding the prohibition of aerial bombardment. The declaration stated that if certain concerns can be avoided, the Japanese delegation can also accept the prohibition of aerial bombardment. The Japanese delegation advocates: 1. The complete abolition of aircraft carriers and the prohibition of installing decks on warships sufficient for aircraft to land. 2. The conclusion of an agreement to prevent the conversion of civilian aircraft for military use in wartime. It stated that it is regrettable that the British disarmament plan has not paid attention to these concerns, as Japan is an island nation and has to prevent various dangers arising from the current situation, while the British plan does not mention a word about whether aircraft carriers should be abolished. The Japanese government believes that the restrictions on the quantity and quality of aircraft carriers in the London Naval Treaty are sufficient to create an atmosphere of unease and fear, and are not sufficient to strengthen the sense of security. Therefore, when making important decisions on the absolute prohibition of aerial bombardment, this situation should be reflected on and hesitated. (Havas, 8th)

Methods for Drawing Aviation Lottery Tickets 61

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance believes that aviation lottery tickets are about to be sold out, and the methods for drawing prizes have been determined by various experts with a meticulous plan to eliminate malpractices. The aviation lottery tickets have fifty numbers. If placed in a ball, the middle numbers would be pressed and sandwiched in the middle and could not be shaken out. Now, three copper round balls are used for the lottery. The first ball contains four-digit numbers, from 1000 to 9000. The second ball contains two-digit numbers, from 00 to 90. The third ball contains the lottery ticket. The first ball shakes out four digits, and the second ball shakes out two digits, totaling one lottery ticket. Then shake the third ball. In this way, there is no way to cheat, and great trust can be shown. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

Japanese Air Force Armory Explodes

Hamamatsu Regiment Burned Down 67

Its Strength is Sufficient to Match a Division and Has Participated in Operations Against Us

Five Consecutive Explosions Turned It into a Sea of Fire

More Than 300 Homes in Nearby Residential Areas Were Completely Destroyed

Hamamatsu, at 8:40 PM on the 7th, the armory of the 7th Flying Regiment in Hamamatsu suddenly exploded. With a loud bang, it destroyed the regiment's barracks and nearby residential buildings. For a time, the entire city was in chaos. At 8:46 PM and 9:35 PM, there were two more explosions, flames soaring into the sky, immediately burning down three armory buildings. The fire brigade rushed to the scene after hearing the news but could not approach. There seemed to be a considerable number of casualties. At 11:50 PM, 500-kilo bombs stored outdoors under the tent were ignited, causing the fourth explosion. At 12:20 PM, there was a fifth explosion, spreading to the volatile oil storage piles. The inside of the regiment became a sea of fire. (Dentsu News Agency, 8th)

Careless Handling of Bombs 68

(Tokyo) According to a report from the Shizuoka Prefectural Office, the reason for the explosion in the Hamamatsu Flying Squadron's armory was that bombs sent from the Okayama Army Ordnance Factory on the 7th were involved in an accident while being transported by twenty horse-drawn carriages. The Hamamatsu Flying Regiment was established in 1925 and is Japan's only bombing regiment. The strength of the regiment is comparable to that of a division. The expenses are huge. It has been dispatched to various battles in Manchuria and Shanghai, undertaking important tasks. This loss is over two million yuan. (Japan United Press, 8th)

Losses Exceed 2 Million 69

(Tokyo) According to the report received by the Army Aviation Headquarters, the No. 1 armory of the 7th Aviation Regiment in Hamamatsu suddenly exploded at 8:35 PM on the 7th. The sound of the explosion shook the entire city. Within an hour, the No. 2 and No. 3 armories also caught fire and exploded one after another. The fire was soaring, and iron and tiles were flying horizontally. The fire brigade did not dare to approach within forty feet. Before long, the gasoline tanks also caught fire. The barracks, aircraft hangar, and aviation school classroom were all engulfed in flames. As of 4:00 AM this morning, 15 soldiers were injured, and two were missing. The fire has not yet subsided. The report received at 8:00 AM this morning is as follows: 1. All three armories were completely burned, and the largest 250 bombs have also disappeared. 2. Two oil tanks and gasoline were lost. 3. Of the 49 aircraft, two heavy and light bombers were burned. The remaining 45 may be safe. The hangar was completely lost. 4. The aviation school buildings and the barracks were completely lost. 5. Fifteen aviation personnel were injured. Kisaburo Nakamura, a director of the aircraft factory, was also seriously injured. The two soldiers who were missing last night have safely returned home this morning. Other losses are not yet clear. (China United Press, 8th)

(Tokyo) According to an investigation by the Japanese Ministry of the Army, the losses caused by the fire in the 7th Aviation Regiment, as of 5:00 PM, in addition to what was announced this morning, include more than 360 homes in neighboring residential areas being burned down. The losses of the aviation team are estimated to be at least 2.5 million yuan. (China United Press, 8th)

In the monarchy era in Spain, from 1834 to 1925, cabinets rarely served a full year. In the ninety years, a total of 113 cabinets were replaced. After that, there was the dictatorship government of Rivera. Since the revolution, the cabinet has only been replaced once in 26 months. The cabinet that resigned today was established in December 1931.

Issues Regarding Reception After the Japanese Army's Withdrawal 74

A Reasonable Plan Has Been Discussed; No Separate Committee Will Be Formed

The Issue of Handling Puppet Troops Still Needs Further Negotiation with the Japanese Side

Sun Dianying's Name Highly Mentioned for Governing Chahar

Special Dispatch from Beiping: Since the signing of the truce agreement, issues such as the withdrawal of the Japanese army and the resolution of the puppet troops have been further discussed by Japanese representatives inviting Chinese representatives, including Xiong Bin, to Tianjin. The Japanese representatives strongly stated that the withdrawal of the Japanese army is not a problem, but due to the complexity of the military branches, the withdrawal must proceed in a certain step-by-step manner, first withdrawing the heavy artillery and supply units, and then gradually withdrawing the forward infantry units. As for the puppet troops, the Japanese representatives suggested that the Chinese side resolve the issue themselves. The Chinese representatives expressed that they were restricted by the agreement and could not use force to resolve it. The Japanese representatives also informally indicated that the police force could be expanded. Detailed measures need to be further discussed after the Japanese representatives meet with the commander of the Kwantung Army, Mutō, in Changchun. Regarding the reception matters after the withdrawal of the Japanese army, some initially suggested forming a reception committee. However, after Xiong Bin and others consulted with Yu Xuezhong, the chairman of the Hebei Provincial Government, they believed that the situation was different from that of Shanghai and that there was no need to form a separate committee. It was decided that the Hebei Provincial Government would take charge. After Yu Xuezhong came to Beiping to discuss the matter with He and Huang, he had already formulated all the plans. Yu returned to Tianjin and can start preparations. Everything is now largely in place. As soon as the Japanese army gradually withdraws, we will gradually take over. The puppet troops in the war zone have been very active in recent days, and the villages east of Lutai have been greatly ravaged. The puppet troops on the Beining Line are mostly concentrated in the Xugezhuang area, with the vanguard only a dozen miles away from Lutai, constantly provoking us. The purpose of the puppet troops is to hope to be reorganized into security teams within the war zone. For the sake of rectifying discipline, the authorities will never incorporate the puppet troops. If the Japanese do not interfere or automatically come up with a solution, we will try to resolve it by force. The number of puppet troops is not very large. Although we are limited by the agreement and cannot send troops to the war zone to suppress them, the police in the war zone can develop their defense rights to maintain local security. Japanese representatives Okamura and others have now arrived in Changchun. It is expected that a solution will be decided within the next few days.

Our army has already withdrawn to the locations stipulated in the truce agreement and does not need to withdraw any further. However, now that the war has stopped, there is no need to station a large army in the north. The transfer of defense and demobilization are being planned. He Yingqin has repeatedly summoned the generals to Beiping to discuss the matter in detail. A reasonable plan has been agreed upon. The first step is to abolish the wartime organization and wartime equipment. The second step is to transfer the defense after the Japanese army withdraws. Now, the wartime serial numbers of each army are gradually being abolished and the original establishment is being restored. All wartime equipment such as military stations and wounded prisoner hospitals are also being closed. As for the defense area of each army, it must be re-designated. A plan has now been set and will be implemented at the appropriate time.

After Feng Yuxiang took office as the Commander-in-Chief of the People's Anti-Japanese Army in Zhangjiakou, the rebel army of Liu Guitang invaded Zhanyuan, and the situation in eastern Chahar suddenly became tense. The authorities are paying close attention to this matter and have decided to take peaceful measures against Feng. Song Zheyuan has long intended to resign from the position of Chairman of Chahar Province. Since Feng has sent Tong Linge as his representative, it is not appropriate to keep the position vacant for long. In recent days, Sun Dianying's name has been highly mentioned for governing Chahar. Under the current circumstances, it is more convenient to have Sun govern Chahar. Since the outbreak of the war, Fu Zuoyi was originally transferred from Suiyuan to Chahar Province. Later, due to the intense fighting at Gubeikou, he was transferred to the Changping area. Now that the war on the Great Wall has ended, the authorities intend to transfer Fu's troops back to Chahar Province to consolidate the border. (June 6th)

Songjiang 77

Midwife Uses Surgery During Childbirth, Mother Dies Tragically

Fang Wangshi, a resident of Hechi Lane in the city, had a daughter named Baobao, who is now twenty years old. She married Wang Xiaohe, a Yue opera performer, as a live-in son-in-law. The couple had a very deep relationship. Baobao became pregnant and felt a slight abdominal pain at 7:00 PM yesterday (the 7th). Xiaohe immediately hired a midwife surnamed Ma from Fenfeng pier to deliver the baby at home. At around 8:00 PM, she went into labor and gave birth to a child. The midwife Ma performed surgery in the hope of removing the placenta. Unexpectedly, as soon as she started, the mother screamed in pain and fainted. What was taken out was not the placenta. The family became anxious and hired another midwife surnamed Chen from the East Gate. Seeing that the incident had already caused a disaster, she refused to start. They then hired Zhang Yuhua, a female obstetrician from Songjiang Hospital, for treatment. Examination revealed that what was taken out was the mother's uterus. It was impossible to save her. She died at 9 o'clock. The midwife's negligence, which caused a person's death, is truly hateful, and the tragic death of the mother is also extremely pitiful.

Wuxi 79

Request to Reduce the Silkworm Stove Business Tax

There are more than 200 silk cocoon firms in this year's spring cocoons. Because the number of fresh cocoons produced recently is scarce, two-thirds of the cocoon scales had stopped operating yesterday. However, the late cocoon is still in a large sleep, so the cocoon line that is left is waiting to collect the late cocoon. In addition, the Cocoon Industry Association stated that the number of silkworm stoves in this county exceeded the amount of cocoon production. The cocoon business has suffered losses for many years, and those who are unable to pay are baking cocoons for farmers. Occasionally, there are merchants who try their best to operate, but they only open three or four silkworm stoves and do not open them to the full capacity. The Education Fund Management Office still needs to pay a tax of one yuan per stove according to the number of silkworm stoves. This is not reasonable. It is now heard that Zhejiang Province has approved a reduction of half the amount collected. Therefore, yesterday, a special report was submitted to the Jiangsu Education Fund Management Office, the Construction Department, and the Wuxi County Government, etc., requesting that it be allowed to reduce the collection of silkworm stove business tax by half in accordance with the precedent in Zhejiang Province.

Military Police Arrest a Society of Big Sword Members 80

Lan Yundong, the commander of the Fifth Regiment of the Wuxi Military Police, recently received a secret order from Commander Gu of Nanjing, stating that according to a secret report, Pu Zhengyang and others, residents of Shitang Town in the 14th district of Wuxi, were recruiting followers in the countryside, purchasing knives and preparing weapons, organizing a Big Sword Society, and plotting wrongdoing. He was ordered to quickly investigate and handle the matter. After receiving the order, Commander Lan dispatched Adjutant Zhang to lead an armed team to the countryside to arrest them. Pu Zhengyang and his eldest son, Shengzu, and second son, Yaozu, were arrested on the spot. Six big swords, one pistol, fifty-two bullets, and two rifles were found in their home. The witnesses were also taken to the city and temporarily detained at the regimental headquarters, pending a formal transfer document to the Nanjing Military Police Headquarters for interrogation.

Cholera Spreads in the Urban and Rural Areas 81

Recently, the weather has been abnormal, suddenly cold and suddenly hot, so there are quite a few people suffering from diseases. Recently, a cholera condition has been discovered in the city again, and the momentum is very strong, and there are quite a few patients. Hua Yushan, who lives in Guanqian Street in the city, also suddenly suffered from the condition yesterday. The family was shocked when they saw it and immediately asked a doctor from a hospital to diagnose and treat it, and he was able to turn the danger into safety.

The Assistant Trial Officer of Chongming is Replaced 82

Xu Shichang, the assistant trial officer of this county, has been in Chongming for only four months. Recently, he was reported for misconduct and for condoning servants to contact the parties concerned in various places, resulting in vague cases and widespread complaints. The people of the county have reported to the Provincial Government and the High Court. The High Court telegraphed to this county earlier this month to transfer Xu to be the assistant trial officer of Danyang County, and the vacancy was replaced by Shen, the assistant trial officer of that county. After receiving the telegram, Xu packed his bags and, on the evening of the 3rd, led his wife and children in the drizzling rain, hired a car to Haihong Port, and took the Beisha wheel to Shanghai.

Zhenjiang 84

Xie Yifang Was Shot and Killed

Xie Yifang, a resident of Fangbian Village in the Third District of the Southern Countryside, previously served as the chief of the security group. Later, he had a conflict with Wu Chengyang, the chief of the Third District, and sued each other in court. As a result, both were injured. Xie was sentenced to two years in prison for embezzlement of public funds, and fined 1,000 yuan. He was pardoned due to the general amnesty. After Xie returned to his hometown from the Suzhou High Court, he trained security guards in the countryside. He was arrested by the county government for another incident. After someone interceded, he was found to be innocent and released. He did not participate in foreign affairs. Unexpectedly, at around 6:00 PM the night before, Xie was having dinner at home when three bandits suddenly came, knocked on the door and entered, claiming that they had official business to see Xie. When he came out to see them, the three men immediately drew their guns and fired two shots, hitting vital points, and he fell to the ground and died. His family heard the alarm and rushed out, but the bandits had already fled. His wife came to the court yesterday to file a complaint, requesting that the murderers be arrested and brought to justice.

A Young Man Came to Hangzhou from Suzhou and Committed Suicide

Fortunately, Shen, a resident of the area, learned of it and took him to the Guangji Hospital for treatment. He is now slightly conscious. When asked about the reason for his suicide, he shook his head and said nothing. His brother, Zhifang, has heard the news and came to Hangzhou from Xiaofeng to visit.

Northeastern People's National Salvation Army

Telegrams Report Arrival in Xinjiang 89

The Scene of the Journey Was Miserable

The Initial Aspiration to Resist Japan Has Never Been Changed

According to the Central News Agency, Wu Tiecheng, the mayor of this city, received two telegrams from the generals of the Northeastern People's National Salvation Army who arrived in Xinjiang from Russia, reporting on the situation in Xinjiang Province and requesting that the relatives of the generals who arrived in Shanghai be informed. The text is transcribed as follows:

Telegram 1

To Mr. Wu Tiecheng of Shanghai and Mr. Zhu Ziqiao, to the representatives of the families of the officers, soldiers, and people of the Northeastern People's National Salvation Army, Du Xinwu, Lin Xueyan, Gu Xuetao, Zhang Datong, Zhao Huichen, Zhao Huichuan, Shen Junru, Fan Zhizhen, and Zhan Jiazhou, greetings. Our troops departed from Domsk on February 23 by train. Supplies were adequate along the way. On the 26th, we arrived at Ayaguz and waited for the Russian side to prepare the sleighs. After staying for three days, we boarded the sleighs and moved forward in the direction of Tacheng. We traveled through snowy nights and were battered by wind and frost. Recalling the miserable scene at the time, we couldn't help but shed tears. On March 8, we finally arrived safely in our homeland, Tacheng County. At that time, we were warmly welcomed by all sectors of the military, political, academic, agricultural, industrial, and commercial circles in the Northwest. The officers and soldiers were all grateful for the help. The people of Xinjiang welcomed us and looked forward to our arrival. We were given prepared vehicles in Tacheng. After staying for two days, we set off. There were special personnel to receive us at the stations along the way. However, the bandits were not at peace and committed petty crimes at night. Fortunately, our troops were able to protect themselves safely. On April 6, we arrived in Dihua. The four gates of the provincial capital were closed, and the atmosphere was bleak. The traces of banditry and devastation were heartbreaking. We are now stationed outside the East Gate, awaiting orders. Unfortunately, on April 12 at 9:00 AM, we encountered a political change in Xinjiang Province. The time was short, and the handling was agile. The merchants and people were unharmed, and the consulate officials were safe. Our troops, based on the doctrine of national salvation, maintained a neutral attitude. The old and new factions had no idle words, and the farmers, workers, and merchants all expressed their goodwill. We are now issuing uniforms and replenishing weapons and ammunition. The officers are carrying out cadre training, and the soldiers are drilling according to regulations, all to boost their fearless spirit and prepare for unfinished work. All our comrades and families can read the telegram to everyone. Our return is not far away, and the time to meet is just around the corner. In view of your remote connection, we send this special telegram to inform you. Signed, Su Guo, Chief of Staff of the 2nd Brigade of the Infantry of the Northeastern People's National Salvation Army.

Telegram 2

To the Tacheng Lu Administrative Director, transferred to the Shanghai Special Municipality Wu Tiecheng and General Zhu, transferred to the representatives of the Northeastern People's National Salvation Army returning to Shanghai from the Soviet Union, Mr. Ren Zuotian, Mr. Du Xinwu, Mr. Shen Junru, greetings. Our brigade departed from Domsk and, thanks to protection along the way, arrived in the Xinjiang provincial capital on March 27 and stopped awaiting orders. The local authorities and elders in Xinjiang welcomed and received us with meticulous care. Please reassure them. The officers, soldiers, and families of our brigade are escorted by your enthusiastic protection and must have arrived in the motherland soon. Our friendship is that of comrades, and our anti-Japanese work has not yet been completed. During this period, there is no need to express gratitude. I only hope that you will take the time to inform all the officers and families of our brigade one by one of the situation of our arrival, so that they may understand the truth and avoid anxiety. I also ask you to protect these orphaned ministers and remnants to the end, so as to avoid displacement. If this is the case, we will be grateful to you for the rest of our lives. I am sending this telegram in a distant spirit, without expressing my full feelings. Zheng Runcheng, acting brigade commander of the 2nd Brigade of Infantry of the Northeastern People's National Salvation Army, knocks on behalf of all officers and soldiers.

Handling Cargo at the Maigen Road Station Changes Hands 95

Official Explanation of Reasons

Labor Union Declaration of Opposition

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Maigen Road cargo station, the railway bureau has canceled the cooperative run by the cargo handling workers on a trial basis, and all cargo handling matters at the station have been contracted to Yang Hengzhen. A reporter inquired with the railway bureau yesterday morning, and the person in charge of the bureau said that the Maigen Road cargo station is the center for cargo transportation on both lines. The railway bureau previously allowed the cargo handling workers to run a cooperative on a trial basis, originally to protect the interests of the workers and the transportation on both lines. However, since the trial began, although there were four foremen, they could neither take responsibility nor manage and restrain the workers. They also did not listen to the station staff's instructions, resulting in the detention of vehicles, control of warehouses, and fighting over work. Such incidents occurred from time to time, delaying cargo transportation for merchants, hindering the safety of railway order, and demanding excessive fees from merchants in addition to the stipulated handling fees. As a result, merchants hesitated to use the station, and cargo transportation at the station has plummeted, causing great losses to the railway bureau. Even the hundreds of workers have difficulty maintaining their livelihoods. Therefore, after several months of investigation and consideration, it was decided to terminate the trial of the cooperative and entrust all cargo handling matters at the station to Yang Hengzhen, who will be solely responsible, in accordance with the Measures for Handling Railway Cargo Loading and Unloading stipulated by the Ministry of Railways. Preliminary contact was made the day before yesterday, and the matter was largely settled yesterday. The railway bureau's announcement and the joint announcement by the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Public Security Bureau, and Security Office are recorded below.

Railway Bureau Announcement 96

Announcement by the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration: Regarding the announcement of cargo handling matters at the Maigen Road Station of this railway, since it was handled by the workers' cooperative, there has been no absolutely responsible representative to preside over it, resulting in a lack of management and restraint. Railway merchants have felt difficulties, and because there are many workers and little work, the supply and demand have been imbalanced. The workers' income is insufficient to maintain their lives, and even the workers themselves must be suffering greatly. This bureau has carefully examined and believes that this situation is extremely dangerous. If it is not rectified urgently, the railway merchants and workers will not be able to easily benefit from it. It has been decided to temporarily entrust Yang Hengzhen to handle and be responsible for the cargo handling matters at Maigen Road Station, so that railway merchants and workers will not have incompatible drawbacks under a complete management system, and there will be mutual benefits. It is hereby announced to all workers at Maigen Road Station to understand the purpose of this bureau. Hereafter, they must follow the methods reported by the contractor Yang Hengzhen and approved by this bureau, and must not deliberately violate them or cause disturbances. This is of utmost importance. This announcement.

Official Announcement 97

Announcement by the Shanghai Municipal Security Office, Public Security Bureau, and Social Affairs Bureau: Regarding the announcement, this is based on a letter from the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, stating that the cargo handling workers at the Maigen Road Station warehouse of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway under the jurisdiction of this bureau had experimentally organized a workers' cooperative in the 17th year (of the Republic), but disputes between workers and merchants have arisen repeatedly, and there has been no end to them. The reason is that the cooperative lacks a responsible representative to preside over it, and there is a lack of management and restraint, resulting in merchants being fearful and avoiding the station, cargo transportation on both lines has declined, and the workers' income is insufficient to maintain their lives due to the large number of people and little work. In the long run, it is not only contrary to the original intention of the trial cooperative, but the workers and merchants are suffering from each other, and the impact on railway transportation and economy is not insignificant. This bureau has carefully examined and believes that industry and commerce cannot cooperate, and the trial has failed. It should be improved urgently. It has been decided to entrust Yang Hengzhen to handle the cargo handling matters at Maigen Road Station and be responsible for rectification. For internal workers, use legal management and control, and for external merchants, use sincere spirit of cooperation, so that both supply and demand can maintain a balance and move towards development together, so that they need each other without hindering each other. Then industry, commerce, livelihood, railway transportation, and social economy will all benefit from it. This move is not only related to the transportation of this bureau, but also to the problem of labor governance in Shanghai. Therefore, the handling of this case will be reported to your office (your bureau) and the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau and Social Affairs Bureau (Security Office and Social Affairs Bureau) (Security Office and Public Security Bureau), and we ask you to issue a joint announcement to persuade the cargo handling workers at the station to listen to the reorganization and not cause disturbances. We sincerely hope for your cooperation, etc., approved. It has been found that the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration's reorganization of cargo handling matters at Maigen Road Station is a great move to increase national income, facilitate industry and commerce, develop social economy, and stabilize workers' lives. It is hereby announced to all cargo handling workers at Maigen Road Station to be fully aware of the sincerity of the railway bureau's reorganization, listen to the restraint of Yang Hengzhen, who is appointed by the railway bureau, and not cause disturbances. If anyone dares to deliberately violate this, report it to the military police nearby for arrest at any time. This is of utmost importance.

Union Declaration 99

The Maigen Road Station Loading and Unloading Branch directly under the Two-Way Union declares that Mo Heng, Director of the General Affairs Office of the Two-Way Administration, led the military police to forcibly cancel the cooperative and restore the contract system. To the Central Party Department, the National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Railways, and to the Silk Party Departments of all provinces and cities across the country, the governments of all provinces, cities, and counties, the special party departments of railways, the railway administrations, the railway unions, the trade unions at all levels in provinces, cities, and counties, all people's organizations, and all newspapers: This loading and unloading branch was established on January 16th, 1929, to undertake the loading and unloading work at the Maigen Road Cargo Station of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways. The Two-Way Administration formulated 30 articles of the Trial Regulations for the Maigen Road Cargo Station Loading and Unloading Workers' Cooperative. The workers have followed the regulations, served diligently for five years, and have been sincere and peaceful to merchants. They have respected and adhered to the Bureau's instructions. All 769 workers have never had any disputes or disturbances. They have assisted the Bureau in transportation and maintained railway production, with merit and no demerit. Since the Ministry promulgated responsible transportation, the cargo transportation on Maigen Road has suddenly decreased. Recently, the workers' daily hard work has earned less than three or four jiao. Under the high pressure of living in Shanghai, the family members are in distress and hardship, and they have not dared to complain. They hope that the cargo transportation will increase in the future, and the workers may have a glimmer of hope. Unexpectedly, at 6:00 am on June 7th of this year, Mo Heng, Director of the General Affairs Office of the Two-Way Administration, suddenly led Zheng, Director of the Transportation Department, Xie Wenlong, Deputy Director of the Transportation Department, He Jingchong, Cargo Inspector, Wang Qiguang, staff member of the Personnel Section, Huang Renjie, Chief of the Police Section, and the entire class of armed railway police, Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau Inspector, and twenty or thirty members of the Shanghai Municipal Security Team, bringing with them contractor Yang Hengzhen to the station, carrying guns and ammunition, with strict security, ordering the branch cooperative to be revoked immediately and handed over to contractor Yang Hengzhen for reception. Director Mo claimed that all workers at the station would listen to the contractor Yang Hengzhen's command in the future. Upon hearing the news, the workers were extremely shocked and could not help but express their opinions to the society, hoping for your consideration. According to the abolition of the contract system and the establishment of cooperatives, it is the consistent policy of our Party to support farmers and workers, and it is also one of the seven movements stipulated by the Central Government. I am especially afraid that the implementation will be ineffective. It has been repeatedly ordered and documents have accumulated. However, Huang Boqiao, Director of this Road, under the leadership of the Kuomintang government, dared to disregard everything, go against the tide, destroy the labor movement, despise the Party, and be harsh to employees. His various improper behaviors are countless and have long been met with resentment. There is no need to hide it. Even with regard to our agency, if there are any inappropriate points, they should also be discussed separately in accordance with the regulations (see Article 28 of the regulations) and be rewarded or punished as appropriate to maintain fairness. But there is no such plan. Now, without education, they are killed. With the section of lightning speed, they led a large number of military police to forcibly hand over. Although the workers are the working people under the leadership of our Party, they are ignorant and do not know whether such actions are the responsibility of the competent authorities under the leadership of the National Government. The workers at this station are subject to the legal supervision and guidance of the stationmaster of this station. Since the agency has undertaken it for five years, all the stationmasters and superiors have never said anything wrong. The responsible leaders can also perform their duties in accordance with the regulations. All the workers at the station have not heard of any violations. The facts are all there and can be seen. Now the Bureau's announcement states that there is no absolutely responsible representative to preside over it, resulting in a lack of management and restraint. I don't know what the basis is. Moreover, the leaders of our agency have already reported to the Bureau for record, guiding the work, with orderly things and unobstructed cargo transportation. How can Director Huang Boqiao cover the world's ears and eyes with one hand? The announcement also says "There are many workers and little work, and the supply and demand are imbalanced." Indeed, but it should be given legal relief in accordance with the revolutionary method, which is the right way to solve it. Now, instead of this plan, it is changed to the contract system, which is tantamount to adding insult to injury and putting our workers to death. Can the supply and demand be adjusted as soon as the contractor is restored? The workers have never heard of it before and should not laugh at it. Moreover, the workers have always sought common welfare in the spirit of cooperation, sharing weal and woe, and living and dying together. How can they seek skin with a tiger? Even if they die, they will have no place to be buried. There are more than 60 stations on both lines, and there are loading and unloading branches directly under the Two-Way Union in each major station. There are organizations of cooperatives in each major station, and there are loading and unloading workers in each small station. Even if the Bureau ignores the Party and the country and wants to restore the contract system and cancel the cooperative, it should also use other methods to seek a solution. It needs the guidance of three directors and the protection of a large number of military police for a small contractor to receive the station, which is the first hearing in the national railway and the new record in the world railway. The majesty of this contractor is really chilling. The above points are just a few of the most important ones. At this time of panic and uncertainty for the workers, on the day when their lives are at stake, in addition to legally submitting to the Party Department and the Union on both lines, and forwarding them to the Ministry and the Central Government for legal disposal, I would like to ask all sectors to uphold public opinion and provide assistance in accordance with the consistent policy of our Party. The workers can only fight to the death with the environment and will never yield. This is a declaration, Zheng Yongxing, Shen Yuqing, Zhang Zichang, and Song Kaigui, the officers of the Maigen Road Station Loading and Unloading Branch directly under the Railway Union of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway directly under the Ministry of Railways, led the fifteen group leaders and all 769 workers to knock.

Shanghai's Exports to the United States Increase 100

Report by the US Consul General in Shanghai

According to the export report compiled by the US Consulate General in Shanghai, the value of goods exported from Shanghai to the United States in May of this year was US$1,055,844, a significant increase compared to the previous four months. The total value of exports in the previous four months was US$2,459,629. The largest number of exports in the five months of this year were inedible animals and animal products, totaling US$1,874,859, of which US$445,855 were in May. The second largest was textiles, with a total of US$1,055,236 in five months, of which US$282,838 were in May. The third largest was non-metallic minerals, with a total of US$300,330 in five months, of which US$272,619 were in May. The remaining items ranged from tens of thousands of dollars to thousands of dollars. The value of goods exported to the Philippines in May was US$110,829, and the total for the five months of this year was US$431,538.

Page 10

Tibetan Merchant Chen Binghui

Discusses Tibetan Politics 103

丨Hoping that the Countrymen Will Strive to Develop the Frontier丨

Mr. Chen Binghui from Songjiang has been doing business in the Tibetan area for more than ten years and is quite familiar with the situation in central Tibet. Mr. Chen arrived in Shanghai from Tibet at the beginning of last month. The reporter met him at a banquet the night before last and he described the recent situation in Kangzang in detail. At a time when the violent Japanese are invading the Northeast and Tibetan troops are attacking Kangqing, it is worth recording, so I will record it as follows.

General Situation of Tibet 104

According to the discussion, the political organization of Mongolia and Tibet are different. Mongolia rules the people with the military, while Tibet rules the people with religion. The Dalai Lama seizes all the power in Tibet. Under him, there are four Gabuluns, who are responsible for religion, politics, military affairs, and finance. Regarding important events in Tibet, they must be decided by the conference of the three major temples of Baiming Temple, Gandan Temple, and Sera Temple. Tibetan people are divided into four classes: monks, nobles, commoners, and slaves. Monks are the most noble because Tibetans all believe in Buddhism. Slaves are the private property of monks and nobles. The disparity in inequality is very contrary to the original purpose of Buddhism.

Urgent Development 105

Tibet has a vast territory and a sparse population. Gold is everywhere, but no one has developed it. The richness of the mineral resources is not inferior to the three northeastern provinces. The wilderness is vast, and there are no traces of people for hundreds of miles. Tibetans have immature knowledge and do not know how to consider this. The number of people from the southeast is very few, which has aroused the coveting of the British. I have traveled to Tibet for more than ten years and feel the following points. I hope the government and the people of the country will pay attention to it immediately so that the western fortress will not be reduced to the second of the three northeastern provinces. 1) Consolidate the border defense; 2) Improve the knowledge of the local people so that they all have the spirit of development; 3) Seek convenience in transportation as soon as possible, such as building roads and installing telegraphs; 4) Encourage compatriots in the interior to go to the frontier to develop wasteland as soon as possible to enrich the strength of the frontier; 5) Pay attention to the drawbacks of ruling the people with religion and seek to liberate slaves as soon as possible.
