US Cotton Loan Does Not Hinder the Yarn Market 107

Statement by Vice Minister Zou of the Ministry of Finance

Daily Newspaper Association Will Host a Banquet for He Huaide Tomorrow Night 108

He Huaide Makes a Statement to Foreign Newspaper Reporters

Mr. He Huaide, Director of the US Scripps-Howard Newspaper Company and Chairman of the Associated Press, recently toured the Far East, passing through Japan to various places in the Northeast and Rehe to inspect the Japanese military's invasion situation. Then he passed through the front line of the two armies to Beiping, visited local officials, and met with old friends. After staying for a few days, he arrived in Shanghai by plane from Beiping the day before yesterday and stayed at the Cathay Hotel. The Shanghai Daily Newspaper Association, considering Mr. He as a major figure in the American press who is concerned about the situation in the Far East and has a lot of goodwill towards our country, has scheduled a banquet for him at Xinghualou on Fuzhou Road tomorrow night, and has invited reporters from various foreign newspapers in this city to accompany him to socialize.

According to the Da Mei Evening News, He Huaide, the Chairman of the American Scripps-Howard Newspaper and the Associated Press, stayed at the Cathay Hotel after arriving in Shanghai yesterday (the 7th). The reporter visited him this morning and was told that he planned to stay in Shanghai for ten days. This trip to the West is to inspect the new developments in the Far East so that the Scripps-Howard newspapers can establish wise and constructive policies based on this. He also said that he may be the first American newspaper editor-in-chief to visit the Far East three times in his life. The Far East will be the center of world news in the next thirty years, and the commercial relationship between the United States and the Far East requires us to thoroughly understand the situation and know the trend of its development. Since the September 18th Incident in 1931, the newspapers of this department have not adopted a malicious policy towards Japan, but a constructive criticism policy, believing that we should not only hold a policy of loud outcry on the Far Eastern situation, but also have an aggressive attitude. He also said that the United States has never had a hostile attitude towards Japan. Since the Manchurian Incident, Japan has regarded the attitude of the United States as anti-Japanese, while China has regarded it as pro-China. In fact, neither is true. The real attitude of the United States is only unwilling to see the peace instruments being maintained destroyed. Years ago, Ford created a very simple machine, which was an adventure in transportation, but today, there is a fine Ford car. The United States regards the Non-Aggression Pact, the Washington Conference Treaty, and the League of Nations Covenant as peace instruments, just like that, unwilling to see them turn to ashes, but hoping that they will have the opportunity to progress and improve, just like the Ford car. However, the United States really made a mistake in 1931 and 1932. Its dealings with the Far East failed to keep pace with the League of Nations. Under the Hoover administration, its activities failed to correspond with other countries. Often, when other countries were actively seeking diplomatic methods to maintain peace in the Far East, the United States stood idly by. When other countries' interest waned, the United States suddenly rose up and jumped to the front line, reminiscent of the high school baseball war. The sudden rise of Hitler to power made Britain and France suddenly feel the need to maintain international covenants and abandon their empty cries. But at this time, Manchuria was already dead, resulting in the current situation. However, the entire situation in the Far East has changed greatly since my last visit, so I decided to come back for inspection to create a friendly and sympathetic news policy that can help each other.

The Jinghu Railway is, in fact, unable to provide passenger cars due to repeated damage to its rolling stock. Apart from the two cars already borrowed from the Pinghan Railway, the remaining eight passenger cars should be provided by the Beining Railway with one first-class sleeping car, one first-class passenger car, one passenger baggage car, one dining car, and one postal baggage combination car; and the Jiaoji Railway should provide three third-class passenger cars for use. This is to be followed immediately."

Repercussions of the Railway Workers' Emergency Loan 116

Representatives Elected to Petition

Request to Revise Three Regulations

Workers and artisans from various departments of the Songnan Zhanghuabang Railway General Factory, due to the severe losses suffered during the January 28th Incident, have been experiencing financial difficulties. They previously submitted a request to the Railway Department, asking it to order the return of their retirement savings (managed by the Welfare Committee), but this was not approved. Subsequently, the Savings Committee resolved to allocate 90,000 yuan from the public reserve fund as an interest-bearing loan for all members. However, upon receiving the "Trial Simple Regulations for Emergency Loans from the Jinghu, Huning, and Hangyong Railway Welfare Savings Association" the day before yesterday, and reading the twelve loan regulations, the workers expressed their opposition. Several articles were considered quite onerous, such as Article 2, which stated that members wishing to borrow must fill out three copies of the application form printed by the association, guaranteed by three members belonging to the same office (same room, same department), and certified by the heads of each department before being submitted to the association's accounting committee for review and processing. Article 9 stated that members who have not borrowed or have repaid their loans may act as guarantors, but during the guarantee period, they may not borrow from the association or act as a guarantor for a second person. According to these two articles, borrowing money by one person would deprive three other people of their borrowing rights, which is too restrictive and lacks universal treatment. What kind of emergency loan is this? Furthermore, Article 4 stated that only those who have served for more than five years can borrow from the association, in units of ten yuan, with a limit of two months' salary, and the total amount may not exceed one hundred yuan. However, the association still reserves the right to refuse payment or reduce the loan amount based on the circumstances. This article is even more contradictory to the needs of poor workers, because railway workers' salaries are based on seniority. The longer the service, the higher the salary grade; the shorter the service, the lower the salary grade. At a time when the cost of living is extremely high, low-level workers are often unable to make ends meet, let alone save money. To impose such strict regulations on emergency loans is to defeat the very purpose of emergency relief. After much discussion, they raised objections and elected Lin Jinlin, Zhu Gengsheng, and Zhang Guilin as representatives to go to Shanghai on Friday (today) to petition the association, requesting the revision of the regulations to provide relief and maintain the well-being of poor workers.

Xiong Xiling Pays Attention to Refugee Children's Education 121

Red Swastika Society Replied Yesterday to Xiong Concurring

Three Ladies of Zhu, Chen, and Ning Donated Over a Thousand Yuan

Xiong Xiling, President of the World Red Swastika Society China General Association, previously noted that refugees in the society's various shelters had nothing to do all day except for two meals. This would be detrimental to their physical and mental health. Furthermore, many of the children had interrupted their schooling due to the war and had come to Beiping to seek refuge. To leave them in such a state of desolation would be a great pity. Therefore, he felt that it was imperative to provide adequate education for the women, children, and refugees in each shelter. Since the Guanghua Temple and Longquan Temple, the second and fifth shelters, had a large number of refugees, with over a thousand people, it seemed appropriate to conduct a pilot program in these two shelters first. The students who had dropped out of school should be taught separately according to their gender. The health of men, women, the elderly, and children should also not be ignored. Technical training should be provided based on their age, physical strength, and weakness. In addition, special maternity wards should be set up for refugee women to give birth, etc. Later, it was heard that Xiong had telegraphed the Beiping General Association, stating that all the instructions had been followed. The refugee school in the fifth Guanghua Temple shelter had been arranged and classes had begun. The refugee school in the second Longquan Temple shelter would also be established soon. There were many talented people among the refugees, including male and female teachers and martial arts instructors, who were willing to teach. Those refugees who did not wish to learn or were unable to learn would be assigned to other work to avoid sitting in the room and becoming pessimistic. The goal was to ensure that the refugees in the shelter forgot that they were war refugees and that the children who had dropped out of school would not abandon their studies. Yesterday, Mrs. Zhu Yazhi, Mrs. Ning Mengyan, and Mrs. Chen Xingya went to visit the society's fifth shelter in Guanghua Temple. They saw that the society's facilities for refugees were very thoughtful and that it paid attention to refugee education by establishing refugee schools. They praised this and donated one thousand yuan specifically for the relief of refugees, and another one hundred yuan for children's books, pens, paper, and stationery, as well as for maternity supplies. It was heard that the ladies had agreed to continue to donate their efforts in the future.

Reason for Early Express Train Delay Yesterday Morning 122

Page 11

Ye Family Garden to Establish Sanatorium

Construction Plan and its Progress 123

Mental Hospital to be Established Near the Garden

Board of Directors Postponed, President Yan in Charge

Sun Yat-sen Hospital to be Constructed on Baseball Field

The news that the Ye Family Garden in Jiangwan had been donated to the National Shanghai Medical College as the Second Practical Sanatorium was reported in yesterday's newspaper. The reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency visited President Yan Fuqing of the hospital yesterday, but he was out on official business, so Mr. Fang Zichuan received the reporter in his stead and described the process in detail, as well as future construction plans. These are now additionally reported above in order to inform the public of the community's welfare undertaking.

Progress Situation 124

According to Mr. Fang, President Yan once served as a professor at St. John's University, and Mr. Ye Ziheng graduated from that school in his early years. Therefore, there was a teacher-student relationship, and the friendship was very deep after he left the school. Mr. Ye was the son of Mr. Ye Chengzhong. When the property was divided, he received an inheritance of about 400,000 yuan. Although he had been managing Shanghai and Hankou for years, he had not made much progress. However, he was still able to preserve the old property and had not incurred any losses. In February of this year, when President Yan and Mr. Ye met, they occasionally touched on current affairs and discussed the medical college and the plan to establish a practical hospital. Mr. Ye, feeling deeply for the country, had been thinking about undertaking public welfare projects to benefit the people. Taking advantage of this opportunity, he generously donated the Ye Family Garden, which occupies more than 80 mu and is worth over one million yuan. When the war in North China became tense, President Yan went north to handle relief matters. When he met with Mr. Ye in Tianjin again, the decision was formally made, but it was limited to the scope of the garden, as Mr. Ye owned the land on both sides of the garden.

Progress Plan 125

However, in order to preserve the inherent garden landscape, President Yan decided that the garden would only house a department of a tuberculosis sanatorium. Work has already begun to repair the original offices, houses, pavilions, and other structures in the garden, and it is expected to be completed by the end of this month, and will be opened first. Although the wards will be divided into grades, the price will be kept as low as possible. On the one hand, President Yan wrote to Mr. Ye a few days ago, asking him to donate another ten or more mu of open space next to the garden to build ordinary wards and neurological wards, as well as public rooms. The construction costs will be raised by the hospital itself. It is expected that a reply will be received within a week, and it is believed that Mr. Ye will readily agree without any problem. The motivation for establishing a special mental hospital is that there has never been such a facility in Shanghai, and that there is a Russian mental health expert named Bailey, who has extensive experience in the study of mental illness. He believes that most of the patients suffering from this disease are caused by excessive stimulation from environmental factors. If they can be placed in a pleasant place and allowed to nurture their bodies and minds in a good environment, the effect will be greater than the power of medicine. Therefore, in order to provide students with practical experience and supplement the city's facilities, it was decided to add the hospital. The equipment used in the sanatorium has been largely donated by the Rockefeller Foundation of the American oil magnate, and some has also been borrowed from the Central Health Department, so everything is very complete.

Board of Directors Postponed 126

After the sanatorium was established, it was originally planned to establish a board of directors to oversee all operations. However, Mr. Ye proposed that President Yan be solely responsible for managing it and that there was no need to establish a board of directors separately. Therefore, the board of directors was temporarily postponed. However, President Yan feared that such a public welfare undertaking could not be the responsibility of one person alone. Therefore, it would be established together with the first teaching hospital of the National Medical College when it was established.

Sun Yat-sen Hospital 127

As for the preparation and progress of the first teaching hospital, it has been planned for three years. President Yan, in order to commemorate Premier Sun Yat-sen, began planning it three years ago. The scale is very large, and the location is selected as the baseball field of the Chinese YMCA on Route Paul Henry in the French Concession, which occupies a total area of 100 mu. School buildings will be built on one side, and a hospital will be built on the other. The construction work is owned by the Rockefeller Foundation of the American oil magnate. A letter has been sent to request a donation, and it is expected that a reply will be received by the end of this month. The construction budget is one million yuan. Before April 18, President Yan had raised about 700,000 yuan from various sources. Once the foundation is determined, fundraising will be conducted to make up the one million yuan budget. The operating fund is also set at one million yuan. The surplus land from the construction of the school buildings and hospital will be used to build a beautiful residence, the income from which will be used to offset the one million yuan fund.

Russian Oil Dumped in China

Oil Merchants Compete by Lowering Prices 128

According to the Guowen News Agency, Russian oil is being dumped in China, leading to price wars. This has had a tremendous impact on the American oil companies Mobil and Asiatic Petroleum and the British oil company Texaco, which previously controlled the oil rights in the Far East. At its peak, gasoline was sold for 1.20 yuan per gallon. Recently, in view of the continuous arrival of Russian oil and the resulting competition, the oil companies have had to lower prices in order to attract customers. Although Shell gasoline from Asiatic Petroleum is selling for 8.5 jiao per gallon, Russian oil sold by Guanghua Company is selling for only 7.65 jiao, which is 8.5 jiao cheaper. The fierce competition in kerosene is unprecedented. The reporter believes that kerosene is closely related to commerce and transportation and that if this situation continues, further price wars are inevitable. Therefore, the reporter visited Guanghua Kerosene Company, which sells Russian oil, to get the details.

Fierce Competition 129

The reporter arrived at Guanghua Company and later met with Director Li of the Gasoline Department. He said that the company had been established for many years, but it had only signed a contract with the Russian Oil Products Corporation to sell Russian oil for about a year. The chairman is Xu Shiying, the general manager is Ke Juchu, and the capital is 3.5 million yuan. The so-called "competition period" has been going on for about four months for kerosene and two months for gasoline. However, during this competition period, the company's business has indeed been thriving. On average, Shanghai, including our company, has four major oil companies. The monthly sales of kerosene are about 12 million boxes (two cans per box), and gasoline sales reach 300,000 gallons. The proportion of kerosene sold by our company accounts for one-quarter, and gasoline accounts for one-sixth. It is indeed remarkable to be able to achieve this number in such a short period of time. As for whether prices will need to be lowered further in the future, it is difficult for anyone to predict. However, the contract between our company and the Russian Oil Products Corporation stipulates two points: (1) Regardless of whether kerosene is expensive or cheap, the oil sold by Guanghua must be cheaper than other oils. (2) No matter how much the price of oil falls or how low it is, the commission must still be maintained. With these provisions, it is no wonder that Guanghua oil is easy to sell, and Guanghua is happy to compete.

Setting Up a Depot and Filing a Lawsuit 130

The reporter then asked about the company's establishment of a depot and its dealings with the Municipal Council. According to Director Li, the company had been selling kerosene for some time, and its oil drums were located in Gaoqiao, Pudong. Recently, in order to expand its business, it planned to build gasoline stations in the local area. When it first requested approval from the Municipal Council, the Municipal Council replied that it was not approved. Later, when it questioned the Municipal Council on the grounds that other companies were able to set up gasoline stations, the Municipal Council replied that it had the right to dispose of the matter. However, outside the prohibited area, other companies and domestic companies were still allowed to set up gasoline stations, but not along the road. The so-called prohibited area includes Avenue Edward VII and Bubbling Well Road. At that time, the company sent another letter to negotiate. The Municipal Council replied recently that it must still abide by its previous proposal. Therefore, the company pointed out that there were other companies' gas stations established in the so-called prohibited area. Since the company's request to establish gas stations was not approved, then other gas stations should also be demolished in order to be fair. Why should the Municipal Council treat them differently? Therefore, the company has hired lawyer Musu to file a lawsuit against the Municipal Council in the Consular Court. The proposed petition will be sent soon. A lawsuit arising from competition in kerosene is about to begin.

After the Increase in Customs Duties

Only Japanese Coal is Abundant 131

Inferior Coal Arrives in Droves

Reduced Price Sales to Chinese Merchants

Since the increase in new customs duties on the 21st of last month, coal has been the most affected of the foreign goods imported into Shanghai. The import customs duty on coal, which used to be 2 yuan per ton, has now doubled to 4 yuan per ton. As the tax has increased, the price of coal has also risen. However, factories and shipping companies that need coal are facing business stagnation and decline. The sudden increase in the price of coal due to the increase in customs duties has greatly reduced their purchasing power. Coal dealers, on the other hand, have too much money tied up in ordering foreign coal to Shanghai. For example, to ship 3,000 tons of foreign coal to Shanghai, the manager has to fill out 40,000 yuan for customs duties and freight alone before the coal can arrive in port. Whether it can be sold is still a question. Therefore, since the 21st of last month, coal brokers in Shanghai have stopped ordering foreign coal. The Hongji, Keelung, Fushun, and other coal mining companies have also stopped shipping coal to China since the 21st of last month because of the high taxes and high prices and the sharp decrease in the demand in Shanghai. In these two weeks, the import of foreign coal has suddenly decreased sharply. Compared to before the increase in customs duties, the import volume is in a ratio of ten to one. Yesterday, the reporter met with people in the industry who said that the suspension of the import of foreign coal was fundamentally due to the increase in taxes and prices, which blocked the way forward. In addition, the market slump has led to the strange phenomenon of foreign coal disappearing today. This has not happened in the past ten years. Since the arrival of foreign coal has stopped in recent days, Kaiping's first, second, and third grade fines have become a necessity in the market. The price per ton is also at 10.78 yuan, and even loading is not enough to meet the demand, resulting in shortages. Japanese inferior coal has seized the opportunity to become active from this month and is being peddled everywhere, willing to reduce prices and only charge between 6 and 7 yuan per ton. In this week, the secret sales of inferior coal to various factories and ships in the middle and upper classes are said to have reached between 300,000 and 400,000 tons. The selling price is less than 7 yuan per ton, which is 3 yuan cheaper per ton compared to the market price. Moreover, all of them are delivered in Shanghai. Not a few Chinese shipping companies secretly purchased the coal. However, Mr. Chen Juntong of Zhongwei Company did not want to be greedy for small gains. In the midst of the activity of inferior coal and the disruption of foreign goods, he spared no expense to order 10,000 tons of Chinese coal, Grade One and Grade Two fines, for the use of commercial ships. This is commendable. Compared to hiring Japanese crew members and using purely Japanese coal on national ships, the difference between the two is really immeasurable. Now, unless there are orders, Hongji, Keelung, and Fushun coal are not shipped to Shanghai. The foreign coal currently being sold on the market is all taxed in the past.

Lu Caibao's Unresting Spirit

Friend's Personal Account of Tragic Death 132

=Teacher-Student Lewdness Causes Bloody Case=

=Cai Bao Has a Spirit, Indeed Captures the Murderer=

On the 28th of last month at 2:15 AM, an unidentified male corpse was found in front of No. 331 Kangti Road in the French Concession, having been hacked to death with an axe. Central Police Station patrol officers Nos. 533 and 700 discovered the corpse. Upon inspection, the body was covered in axe wounds, with 23 cuts, and eight stab wounds from a small knife. An axe with a broken wooden handle was found on the ground about one door away from the body, facing west. The detective took the axe back to the police station for evidence. The body was transported to the morgue. As no family members were found, the case was reported to the Second Special Court Prosecutor for examination. It was ordered that the body be buried by the Tongren Fuyuan Hall. The French police arrested an accomplice in the case, who was sent to court yesterday for interrogation. The case arose from adultery and is quite complex. The following is a record of the causes of the tragedy, and the solving of the case.

A Section of Rice Letter Account 133

The following is the interrogation: The deceased, Lü Caibao, was 22 years old, from Ninghai, Taizhou, Zhejiang. Correcting Reduced Sentence Cases

Filing Extraordinary Appeals 143

=The Supreme Court Orders Compliance=

=Major Errors to Be Sent to the Department for Review=

The Procuratorate of the Local Court of this city yesterday received an instruction from the Procuratorate of the Jiangsu High Court, which was transferred from the Procuratorate of the Supreme Court, stating that since the promulgation of the Amnesty Ordinance, there have been many errors in the cases of reduced sentences tried by courts in various provinces. This Procurator has filed extraordinary appeals to correct them, and the judgments have been published in the Gazette of the Judicial Yuan. However, as time has passed, such erroneous cases have not decreased. The number of extraordinary appeals filed by prosecutors in various provinces has been increasing day by day, and they are all being filed case by case, which is both labor-intensive and uneconomical. Therefore, in addition to issuing orders, the Prosecutor is ordered that in cases of reduced sentences, except for major errors, which should still be sent to this Department for review, those with similar sentencing periods or that are clearly not detrimental to the defendant, should not be filed for extraordinary appeals to save the trouble of paperwork, and all subordinates should be ordered to comply. Having received this, in addition to issuing separate orders, the Prosecutor is ordered to comply.

Sun Peijia Experienced Hardships Since Childhood

Again Sighing That She Married the Wrong Person 144

=Her Husband Actually Commits All Kinds of Evil=

=Sun Can Hardly Endure and Asks for Divorce=

Sun Peijia, a woman from Guilin, Guangxi, is 36 years old this year. She lost her parents in childhood. A British female missionary, Miss Heng, saw that she was lonely and helpless and took her in, bringing her to Shanghai. She first studied at the Xinde Society Church School on Jessfield Road, and then changed to the Bayijiang Ai Yu Girls' School. After she graduated, she was assigned to teach at the Xinde Society. In September of the tenth year of the Republic of China, through the introduction of a Mr. Zhang, she married Sun Boying, a native of Haining. Later, she learned that Sun was a rascal with no legitimate occupation. Sun also deceived Miss Sun, saying that he was working in the police station as a police officer with a monthly salary of thirty yuan and that he hoped to be promoted in the future. However, Sun Boying completely ignored household expenses, which were entirely supported by his wife's teaching income. In September of the twelfth year of the Republic of China, Sun Boying was arrested for impersonating a police detective, illegally searching opium in a resident's home on the grounds of extortion. He was sentenced to one year in prison by the court. During this period, he was also reprimanded by his in-laws. After Boying completed his sentence and was released from prison, he had an affair with another woman and often extorted money from his wife. Peijia resented her bad fate and introduced him to jobs, but he was not content in any position. Unexpectedly, in recent times, Sun Boying, in addition to ordering Peijia to borrow money everywhere for his squandering, also used Peijia's name to swindle gold and silver ornaments and silver dollars from her classmates, causing great damage to her reputation. Such behavior was intolerable and it was impossible to grow old together. She hired Lawyer Yu Enliang to file a lawsuit in the First Special District Local Court, requesting that she be granted a divorce. Yesterday morning, Judge Li Hu opened the court for questioning. The defendant could not be served because the address was unknown, so he did not appear in court. The plaintiff, Sun Peijia, explained the situation. The judge ordered that the case be adjourned and the defendant be summoned again for questioning.

New Initiatives by the French Concession Public Works Bureau Fire Department 147

Equipped with Mobile New-Style Rescue Machine

To Rescue Those Who Are Suffocated, Drowned, or Electrocuted

The Fire Department of the Public Works Bureau of the French Concession of this port is now equipped with a rescue machine that can save people who are suffocated, drowned, or electrocuted. This machine consists of an automatic artificial respirator, which can avoid the difficulty of manual breathing. This device is called Panis and a metal mask, which covers the mouth and nose to assist artificial respiration and inhale oxygen. This mask is called Nicloux. Whenever there is an emergency, please contact the Xiafei Road Fire Station or call 80100, and a rescue vehicle can be dispatched with this machine to the scene for rescue.

Reader's Consultant

Love, Reading, and Saving the Nation by Qing Lou 163

| Zhang Jishi from Taicang wrote |

Editor:

I am a modern normal school student, and I am a skeptical person. Whenever I encounter something, I assume that I can understand it, and then I'm done with it. If I have any doubts, I either ask the teacher or discuss it with my classmates. Sir, today I have something to ask about. This matter is not extremely important, nor is it something that teachers and classmates cannot answer. It is truly because the more they answer for me, the more my doubts increase. Therefore, I have no choice but to ask you!

Last night, I received a letter from an old classmate of mine who is studying in Suzhong Province. At the end of the letter, he signed himself as Xiaoman. He is not only my old classmate but also my old fellow townsman. After reading a small section of this letter, my questions arose.

A passage in his letter said, "Since Mei Mei abandoned me three months ago, and I have also suffered from being cheated in love by a female scammer (fortunately, old friends are just talking about it), my spirit has been decadent, and my behavior has become increasingly eccentric. Recalling the past, I often pushed books away and wept all day long, so I changed my name to 'Canshou' and 'Xiaoman,' taking the meaning of taking away what I loved."

Sir, regarding this small passage, I suddenly have many doubts. Now I will briefly write a few points below:

(1) We young students, in the current environment, can we still talk about the word "love"? And are these tasks that young people should be rushing to do now?

(2) Is it the spirit and will that young students should have if they become spiritually decadent and their behavior becomes increasingly eccentric because of a valueless setback?

(3) "Often pushing books away and weeping all day long," is this love more important than reading, especially in the current situation, and under the saying "Saving the country requires reading, and reading is saving the country"?

(4) Is this kind of person a decadent, weak person who cannot stand in the current environment in the current environment?

Sir, I hope you will answer me in detail, and at the same time, you can also give Canshou a compass in the vast ocean of confusion. I am extremely grateful!

Answer: We only regard love as the same as eating and dressing, but there is a difference: If you don't eat for a day, you will be hungry; if you don't wear clothes for a day, you will be cold, but you will never die if you don't fall in love for three to five years. Now that the country is destroyed and the family is ruined, a group of people with power and money are promoting entertainment there, naturally with other intentions. However, if you, as a group of young people, are truly unwilling (in action, not just in words) to be slaves of a fallen country, you must unconditionally put aside this useless activity and do the work of saving the country. If you truly encounter female warriors with the same aspirations in the work of resisting Japan and anti-imperialism, and you unite with each other to fight together, advancing shoulder to shoulder and dying side by side in the face of the enemy, that is a real man. This is the first point.

If you suffer a little setback, you will become spiritually decadent, and your behavior will become eccentric. This kind of young people are called "three-year-old elders." What "spirit and will" can they talk about? This is the second point.

"Pushing books away and weeping" is what is called "blood flowing from the eyes and ashes forming in the heart," which is of course unacceptable. Generally speaking, "reading" is naturally more important than "love." However, if you take what you quoted, "Saving the country requires reading, and reading is saving the country," which is a new metaphysics, then reading and love are actually about the same, half a catty on one side and eight taels on the other. Because talking about love must still carry a little emotion. Today, when the enemy has entered our house, we are still superstitious about the empty theory of "saving the country by reading," which is truly irrelevant. "The son of a thief," "destroying your country," "will the ghosts of the Ruo'ao clan not be hungry?" Japanese imperialists will inevitably sneer at us, saying: "Slave! This is the third point. What is the need to say about the fourth question? No further answer!

Free Talk

Another Meaning of Religious Superstition 164

— Da Wu

The progress of human civilization is often uneven and contradictory. For example, Shanghai people today know how to use airplanes to save the country, but last year's newspapers still reported that an airplane crashed in a mountain in Liling, and the villagers burned incense and kowtowed to it. The recognition of the same airplane differs so much. It is easy to explain that villagers in the countryside have shallow knowledge, a low level of culture, and naturally more superstition. However, the same goal of saving the country leads some to use airplanes, while others go to the Shuilun Buddhist ceremony to pray for peace, or to the patriotic gathering to try to avert national disaster. It is not easy to understand that logic. But this does not mean that patriotic gatherings cannot save the country, or that Buddhist ceremonies are useless for peace. A modern woman with high heels might go to the City God Temple to burn incense and pray for a child, and it might be quite effective as long as her husband does not die. However, even today, superstition can still grip the minds of our masters and madams so tightly, which shows the great power of religion. No wonder that while the national crisis is raging, temples in some places are being hastily renovated, and Buddhist statues in some places are busy being gilded. And recently, Shanghai's masters and madams, after "a hundred years," are also keen on having monks and Taoists putting on a funeral procession, with a lineup that stretches for one or two streets, believing that it is a glorious farewell after death.

It is said that religion originated from primitive people's inability to understand "nature" but their need to rely on it for survival, leading them to doubt, then to marvel, then to worship, and then to pray. This mentality has become today's City God, the Bodhisattva, the gathering for national salvation. But humankind today is no longer the same as humankind in the past, and the relationship with "nature" is vastly different: in the past, they had to eat raw meat and drink blood, but today they can sit in a car and comfortably go to Da San Yuan or Yizhi Xiang to eat Chinese and Western cuisine. Even if it cannot be the same for everyone, at the very least, it does not come down to taking raw wild things and feeding them directly into the mouth. The ability to recognize "nature" is of course a million times greater than that of primitive people. However, why is it that the tricks of the barbarian era can still remain until now, and never decline, like the pigtail worn by a coolie on his head, shamelessly exposed in the street? It is difficult to explain this logic. You should know that those who are the most superstitious are often those with the highest level of culture and knowledge in society, who must ride in cars when they go out, live in foreign houses when they enter, eat rich and thick meals, and employ the most "natural" power. Stupid men and women can only follow behind them, kowtowing and bowing.

Going to fortune-telling or character analysis behind the City God Temple or near the Great World, what they are praying for is not rain for the world, but rather seeking success in their careers, and hope for prosperity. In between, the relationship with "nature" has decreased, and the prayer for social affairs has increased. It is not difficult to know that the psychology of religious superstition is now not only the meaning of dealing with "nature."

Those in power want to use this mentality to solve personnel problems, and those below can only use this mentality to hope for luck. The problem of religious superstition cannot be as easily solved as the great writer Goethe said: with "science," "science," and "art," there is no need for religion. Simply changing "nature" is not enough for the progress of human civilization.

View of Death 165

— Tang Tao

About two or three years ago, Liang Yuchun raised the question of the view of death, hoping that everyone would discuss it, but scholars seemed to hate that Liang forgot their "truths that they fought hard for," so they did not respond, so that there is still "death" without "view," or there is "view" but not for "death."

People all know, but do not often think about, on the edge of life, on the other side of the universe, there is "death." From the womb to the tomb is such a short road, Gao Lei (Abraham Cowley 1618-1667) once called it a Pas de Vie, like Pas de Calais; yes, life is like a narrow strait, we cannot predict the arrival of death, maybe every day can be our last day! Death gives us the opportunity to see our own faces clearly, and we must also see the face of death.

Death should not be terror. Half a year ago, my close friend suffered from heart disease. On a quiet winter afternoon, quietly, he left this world: not half a word, nor a trace of pain, he just lay quietly; the eternal farewell made me go from sobbing to wailing, but I believe that death is not terrible.

But I have also seen the hideous death. A wounded coolie in the neighborhood groaned in pain day and night, suffocating, struggling, until he took his last breath; his whole body convulsed at the time of his death, his eyebrows locked, his mouth open, clearly a painful phenomenon.

But what the peaceful death and the hideous death gave me was the same skull.

Everyone is a skull, but what does the skull imply to us? Perhaps there are still thoughts of wealth and loss existing in the hollow head, perhaps the love and hatred of the world are still hanging in the exposed teeth, or perhaps everything is reduced to nothing, the universe forgets him, and he forgets the universe.

We are still holding on to this life and studying death from the standpoint of life. We cannot find news of the country of death. In the mouth of the witch doctor,

What we get is just a situation similar to the human world, these ghosts (if there are any) are dreaming human dreams, speaking human words, and not the real news of the country of death.

Yuchun is dead; maybe he is still studying this issue, but he can no longer tell us his insights.

We are all mortals who will die. If we say "death lives on in the memory of the living," then I can finish here.

Random Remarks from Qulu, Part 40 166

— Yang Zhuangyuan (Foreign Graduate)

There is a commentary in the first issue of Min Bao titled "How Ugly is Jin Bangping," which roughly said that the Manchu government used its means of controlling people's hearts, so there was the act of the palace examination for students studying abroad. Jin Bangping was the one who sorrowfully initiated it. On the birthday of the Manchu chief, the Manchu slave Yuan Shikai held a grand banquet in Tianjin, inviting consuls from various countries to celebrate the Manchu chief's birthday. He also gathered students from Tianjin to celebrate. Thousands of people attended on that day. Shikai personally encouraged the students in the language of slaves. When the meeting was about to end, suddenly one person went on stage and said to the crowd, "Do you all know me? I graduated from studying in Japan, and I am grateful for being awarded the position of Compiler of the Hanlin Academy. I am not worth mentioning, but the Holy Grace is so great, enough to show that the court values students. I encourage you all, don't worry about not being like me." Everyone looked at him, and it was Jin Bangping. Not long after the meeting ended, Bangping rode in a sedan carried by four people, with two plaques listing his titles, one for "Granted Jinshi Background" and the other for "Appointed Compiler of the Hanlin Academy," parading ostentatiously through the city. People all looked sideways and whispered to each other, "This is the foreign graduate!" It is noted that Min Bao was first published in 1905, which is the 31st year of Guangxu. More than eight years later, the Manchu Qing Dynasty was destroyed. Alas! Cities sometimes become lakes, and seas sometimes become fields; floating clouds in the sky are like white clothes, and in a moment they change into blue dogs; who among the reporters of Min Bao would know what would happen thirty years from now? In the past, Jin Bangping did not seem to be worth despising, but now the rampant people are everywhere, and they are not limited to students studying abroad. The one who created Jin Bangping was the Manchu Qing government. What is there to blame in Jin Bangping? If the reporters of Min Bao were still alive, would they also agree with me? The collected edition of Min Bao is titled "Psychology Textbook" to avoid the ears and eyes of the Manchu Qing government. At that time, the Manchu Qing government was too violent to approach, but where is it now? I sigh three times and put down my pen for it.

Editor's note: Yesterday, I received a letter from Mr. Zizhan, who is now focusing all his efforts on a certain work and has no time for other things. The Random Remarks from Qulu will end here.

Seven Days in a Hospital Bed 167

— Ms. Xiong Xiang

May 19th

I moved into the hospital this afternoon. When I came for a diagnosis this morning, the doctor said: It's really fortunate that I haven't died yet. I repeated this to Ming Ge when I got back, and Ming Ge was startled and immediately forced me to stay in the hospital. But I was a little unwilling. First, I had to leave my Ming Ge, who was like my hands and feet, and second, staying in the hospital would increase his burden. Besides, it's so lonely in the hospital!

May 20th

I woke up at about 2 AM. I had a dream that was quite unpleasant. The person I resolved to forget inexplicably came to my mind again. It was very uncomfortable. In the dream, I heard that Liansheng and Duan Jie had gotten married. I went to see Sister Chun, but she wasn't home. I took the opportunity to visit the newly married Duan Jie. Duan Jie only told me to leave. Liansheng hurriedly ran over to hold me back, not letting me go. His attitude was very ugly. After waking up, the dream was still vivid, and it was very painful. I just wanted to find a knife to cut the pain out of my heart.

I waited from 5 AM until Ming Ge finally staggered in at 2 PM. Jing Ge followed behind him. Now I have finally tasted the pain of longing, which is even worse than usual when I'm sick.

This is my first time staying in a hospital. As soon as I came in, I learned that I had to call the nurses "Miss," otherwise, I would be blamed. I never thought that there would be such a noble title here.

There are six beds in the room. Including me, there are five patients lying in them. One is from Shaoxing, one is from Hubei, one is from Jiangxi, and one is from Guangdong. We call each other by our place of origin. My neighbor is from Guangdong. I heard that she had surgery, so her illness is the most serious. She lies silently all day long. I am the least sick among the five, so I am also the most active. I can get out of bed and walk around, and I can do everything myself without having to ask the nurses for help. Presumably because it's a third-class ward, the nurse only comes to make the bed, check the temperature, and give medicine once a day. The Guangdong woman's copper bell at the head of the bed often rang for a long time without anyone appearing. Sometimes I hear voices from the next room, and the patients quickly shout, "Oh, Miss..." The response is sometimes none, sometimes: "Okay, I'll be there in a minute." As a result, they either come, or they don't come at all. The patients often shout until they cry, but outside, you can often hear the laughter of the Misses and the tea boy. I can't figure out how the people in the hospital are trained to be so cruel. The hospital is really like a battlefield. However, in the first-class wards next door, you never hear the patients calling. Humanity's cruelty to humanity also has first-class and third-class distinctions.

May 21st

Ming Ge can only accompany me for half a day. He was quite reluctant to leave. After he left, the people in the room started a discussion. The Shaoxing woman said, "You two are very close, very intimate." The Hubei woman said, "The closer you are, the more diseases you will have." They are mostly people who work in factories, and no one comes to visit them all day long. The hospital is like society. Most of the people who are sick in the third-class ward are lonely and helpless people. No matter where you go in this society, the classes are clearly divided and will not be confused. (To be continued)

Red Carrot Whiskers 168

— By Jules Renard, translated by Lin Qu

Plum

After tossing and turning on the feather bed for a while, the godfather said, "Beast, are you asleep?"

Red Carrot Whiskers: No, Godfather.

Godfather: I'm not asleep either. I'm awake. If you'd like, let's go catch worms together. "That's a good idea," said Red Carrot Whiskers.

They both jumped out of bed, got dressed, lit a lantern and ran into the garden.

Red Carrot Whiskers held the lantern, while the godfather held a tin box containing half a box of wet mud. The box stored some fishing worms. The surface was covered with a layer of moist moss, so the worms would never run out. After a whole day of rain, the harvest was very considerable.

"Be careful not to step on the worms," he said to Red Carrot Whiskers, "walk gently. If I weren't afraid of catching a cold, I'd rather take off my shoes and walk in socks. As soon as they hear a little noise, the worms will dart into their holes. But we can only catch them when they are far from their holes. We have to grab them suddenly and hold them a little tighter to prevent them from slipping away. If half of their body has already burrowed into the hole, then let them go: otherwise, you will break them. And broken worms are of no use at all. And they will also cause other worms to rot, and refined fish will not bother to eat this kind of rotten worm. Some fishermen are stingy with their worms, which is really wrong. If you don't use whole, live, wriggling worms, you won't catch good fish. Because the worms are moving in the water, the fish think they are going to escape, so they rush to swallow them without hesitation."

"I can never catch them," Red Carrot Whiskers grumbled, "my fingers get dirty with their disgusting saliva."

Godfather: Worms are not disgusting. Worms are the cleanest things in the world. They only eat dirt, and if we squeeze them, they will just turn back into dirt. As for me, I could put them in my mouth and eat them.

Red Carrot Whiskers: As for me, I'd rather let you eat them. Please eat them and show me.

Godfather: These worms are a bit too big. And you have to fry them first, then spread them on bread to eat. But small ones, like the worms inside plums, I can eat raw.

Red Carrot Whiskers: Right, I know. That's why I make my family dislike you, especially Mom, who feels like throwing up when she thinks of you. As for me, I agree with you but don't imitate you, because you have a good temper and we get along very well.

He raised the lantern, climbed down a plum tree, and picked some plums. He kept the good ones for himself and handed the worm-eaten ones to his godfather. The godfather took them, swallowed them whole with the pit, and said:

"These are a few of the best tasting ones."

Red Carrot Whiskers: Ah! Even I want to put them in my mouth and eat them like you. But I'm afraid my mouth will smell bad, and I'm afraid Mom will scold me when she hugs and kisses me.

"There's no smell at all," said the godfather, breathing on his godson's face.

Red Carrot Whiskers: Really. Your mouth only smells of smoke. I can smell that right away. Godfather, I like you very much, but if you didn't smoke, I would like you even more.

Godfather: Beast! Beast! Smoking is good for your health.

Middle School Examination in Fujian Province in Late This Month 171

The Anti-Tide Has Subsided

Fuzhou Correspondence The Fujian Provincial Department of Education will divide the graduating class students of middle schools throughout the province this year into nine examination districts. Each district will form an examination committee, with the county education bureau chiefs, education department supervisors, and principals of middle schools serving as members. The examination is scheduled to begin in late June. However, the graduating class students of middle schools are extremely opposed to this. Students in Fuzhou, Xiamen, Zhangzhou, Quanzhou, and Xinghua have organized a joint committee, established a resident office in the province, united as one, expanded the movement, and issued a declaration, putting forward four points: ㈠ There is no uniform standard for the curriculum of each school. Although they are all in the general course, the school authorities, in order to suit the personality of the students and the special nature of the school itself, often emphasize a certain subject or adopt a student elective system. The subjects stipulated in the examination method are neither divided into subjects nor are they selected. What we have studied and what the Department of Education examines are obviously different. ㈡ According to the regulations of the examination method, "those who fail in one subject in the examination will not be allowed to graduate," and it is also stipulated that it will not be averaged with the grade scores of the above semesters. It is the intention of education to issue test questions without any standard, and to determine scores without any standard basis. If there is a slight error, three years of effort will be in vain. ㈢ The promulgation of the examination method was not at the time when we entered school, but two months after the beginning of our six semesters of study. We were not given sufficient time to prepare, and we must also test the coursework of the past two years. Our energy is limited, and our time is limited. Within this short period, even if we want to burn the lamp and continue the day, we cannot do it. ㈣ According to the Department's statement, the two courses for the graduation examination are handled in accordance with the orders of the Ministry, and were already announced in the 19th year. Why did the previous two examinations only test the coursework of one semester, while this year there is a difference? However, the attitude of the Department of Education is also very strong, and it has sent telegrams to the examination committees of each district, stating that they are allowed to use coercive measures to suppress students' opposition. Any student who does not participate in the examination alone will have their graduation qualification revoked. If the entire class does not participate in the examination, the entire class will be disbanded. If there is any riotous behavior, the local public security bureau will be notified to send police to arrest and investigate the case. Any student representative who goes to the Department to petition will be rejected. Therefore, the graduating class students of middle schools in Fuzhou, Xiamen, Zhangzhou, Quanzhou, and Xinghua have all gone on strike, and are carrying out a province-wide strike to resist. The situation is quite serious. The day before yesterday, Liu Aiqi (manager of Fuzhou Electric Company) and other parents of students took the responsibility of mediation. The Department of Education also feared the expansion of the tide, and began to agree to handle the matter in a flexible manner within the scope of not conflicting with the orders of the Ministry. On the one hand, Liu and others persuaded the students to go to class first and wait for the Department's orders to be implemented. The opposition to the examination problem came to an end here. (June 5th)

Eliminating Misunderstandings Among Some Private School Teachers

Strictly Cracking Down on Resistance Movements

The Department of Education of Jiangsu Province, because the reform of private schools is an important policy, is actually seeking opportunities for private school teachers to survive, and for private school children to obtain the right way to study. It is reported that the Department of Education, in view of the fact that after the propaganda week was held, most of the private school teachers have been able to wake up and accept the opinions of the administrative authorities, and jointly seek reform methods, while there are still a few stubborn people who have not changed their old ways. Moreover, in the provincial capital, there are some private school teachers who intend to unite and resist. Jiangsu Province Holds Higher and Ordinary Qualification Examinations 175

The Department of Education Organizes an Office to Prepare Everything

The Registration and Examination Dates Are Separately Scheduled

Jiangsu Province has planned the examination dates for the higher and ordinary qualification examinations, and has sent them to the Examination Committee for transfer to the Examination Yuan for review and approval, and has requested the dispatch of the Chairman of the Examination Committee (usually the Director of the Department of Education) in the case. It is now learned that the Central Government has issued the appointment of the chairman of the committee to the Department of Education, and is planning to organize an examination office to start preparations. It is also learned that the higher qualification examination will be held from July 20 to the end of July, and the ordinary qualification examination will be held from August 5. The registration dates for the two examinations are also scheduled from June 10 to July 10. All those who wish to take the examination should prepare four two-and-a-half-inch portraits, a registration fee of two yuan, and a letter of guarantee from a public official above the level of commissioner in this province, or a teacher above the level of middle school, and register in person at the examination office set up by the Department of Education. However, those who are far away and unable to come in person can entrust someone with the above qualifications to register on their behalf. Those who have been examined and have obtained a qualification certificate for a subject, after verification, will be exempted from the examination of the qualified subjects. If you want to send a letter to request various regulations, registration instructions, certificates, etc., you must pay five cents for postage, in order to send a reply.

Ministry Order to Pay Attention to Issuance by the Judicial Yuan

Certificates of Graduation for Law Students 176

The Ministry of Education has issued a circular to the national universities, independent colleges, and private universities with law departments and the relevant education departments, stating that "It has been approved by the Executive Yuan in Instruction No. 2377 that 'It has been approved by the Judicial Yuan that, according to Article 15 of the Regulations on the Supervision of the Law Department of National Universities promulgated by the Judicial Yuan, "The Law Department of National Universities shall follow these regulations, and those who are deemed to have excellent academic performance by the Judicial Yuan shall be issued a certificate by the Judicial Yuan when the students have completed their studies and passed the examination." Furthermore, Articles 16 and 17 state that "These regulations shall also apply to provincial, municipal, and private universities and independent colleges." There have been many cases in recent times where schools have requested the issuance of certificates of graduation for law students, but they have often failed to comply with the requirements of these regulations regarding the submission of course schedules and the request for supervision of examinations. Since the academic performance has not been assessed by this Yuan, certificates cannot be issued hastily. In order to strictly enforce supervision, the Judicial Yuan has formulated five rules for the issuance of certificates of graduation for law students, which will be promulgated separately by Yuan Order. A copy is hereby copied and sent to your Yuan for your information and transmission to the Ministry of Education to notify all universities or independent colleges with law departments to comply with these rules, and to order them to pay attention to Articles 6, 7, 8, and 14 of the regulations, which must be strictly followed and not treated as mere formalities, in order to comply with the law and facilitate assessment.' The original rules are copied and issued to the Ministry of Education for compliance by all universities. This order."

Rules of the Judicial Yuan for the Issuance of Certificates of Graduation for Law Students

Article 1: These rules are formulated in accordance with Article 15 of the Regulations on the Supervision of the Law Department of National Universities by the Judicial Yuan. Article 2: National universities or independent colleges with a law department that have complied with the provisions of Articles 6, 7, 8, and 14 of the Regulations on the Supervision of the Law Department of National Universities by the Judicial Yuan, and have been deemed to have excellent academic performance by the Judicial Yuan, may submit a list of graduates from the law department and request the issuance of certificates. Article 3: National universities or independent colleges requesting the issuance of certificates shall submit the graduation certificates and grade transcripts of each student to the Judicial Yuan for review, and shall pay a certificate fee of three yuan and a stamp duty of five jiao for each certificate. Article 4: These rules shall also apply to provincial, municipal, and private universities or independent colleges requesting the issuance of certificates. Article 5: These rules shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

Ministry Order on the Hiring of Party Ideology Teachers 177

The Ministry of Education has issued a circular to the education departments of all provinces, stating that "It has been approved by the Central Executive Committee's Guidance Committee on Mass Movements that, according to the Tianjin Municipal Party Ideology Research Association of Primary and Secondary School Party Ideology Teachers, please forward a letter to the Ministry of Education to order all primary and secondary schools under its jurisdiction not to cancel the Party Ideology curriculum during this semester, and not to hire Party Ideology teachers who have passed the examination. etc." It is stipulated that the primary schools of all grades should start to implement them uniformly from the 22nd academic year, and the junior and senior high schools should start to implement them from the 22nd academic year for the new enrollment first grade. Students in each grade who entered school before the 22nd academic year should still implement teaching according to the temporary standards of the middle school curriculum. Therefore, the Party Ideology subjects should still be preserved in the 32nd grade of each grade of primary and secondary schools and the 22nd grade of junior and senior high schools and the 23rd grade of junior and senior high schools this semester, and Party Ideology teachers who have passed the examination should be hired. The above is approved in the letter. In addition to replying to the letter, it is urgent to order you to comply with it. This order."

It is also reported that the Ministry of Education has telegraphed Xiamen University that schools above the specialized subject level should still add Party Ideology courses as usual.

The Municipal Education Association Actively Carries Out the One Yuan One Month Education Movement 183

The Outline of the Measures for People's Schools Was Published Yesterday

Since the Shanghai Municipal Education Association launched the One Yuan One Month Education Movement, it has been actively carrying out its work without sparing any effort. The outline of the measures for people's schools was published yesterday as follows: Article 1: The purpose of people's schools is to follow the educational objectives of the Republic of China and its implementation policies, and to impart simple knowledge and skills to illiterate adults so that they can adapt to social life. Article 2: The principle of people's schools is to be run directly by the association. However, when necessary, the district education association may be entrusted to run them on its behalf. The name of the people's schools directly run by the association shall be determined by the association, and the teachers and staff shall also be appointed by the association. Article 3: All illiterate men and women between the ages of sixteen and fifty may enter people's schools (the number of students enrolled in each school shall be determined by the association according to the economic situation). Article 4: Students of people's schools shall fill in a letter of guarantee with a guarantor upon entering the school (the letter of guarantee stipulates that if the student is expelled or withdraws from school for no reason, the guarantor shall compensate the association for the loss of one yuan per month, in order to show restriction). (Article 5: The number of students in each class of people's schools shall be 30 to 50 as the standard. Article 6: The textbooks for people's schools are as follows: literacy, writing, daily common sense, arithmetic or pen calculation, music and songs, and other shallow reading materials may be taught according to the needs of the environment. Article 7: The textbooks used by people's schools shall be those approved by the Ministry of Education, and shall be purchased and distributed by the association together with other supplies. Article 8: The duration of study for people's schools shall be four months, with at least twelve hours of classes per week. The time may be in the morning, afternoon, evening, or on holidays. Article 9: Students of people's schools who have completed their studies and whose grades are passing shall be given a graduation certificate by the school. Article 10: People's schools shall hold a weekly meeting once a week, and may hold lectures, exhibitions, or promote proper entertainment outside of class. Article 11: The school buildings and equipment of people's schools shall be limited to the use of existing equipment in schools at all levels and public places. Article 12: Students of people's schools shall be exempt from tuition and other fees, and all books and stationery used shall be provided by the school. Article 12: The budget standard for the expenses of people's schools shall be determined separately. Article 14: People's schools shall, at the beginning and end of each week, submit a list of students, a general overview of the school, and a list of graduates and their grades in accordance with the forms prescribed by the association for review and approval. Article 15: People's schools shall fill in and record the attendance and reasons for withdrawal of students in accordance with the prescribed forms every week, and submit them at the end of the month for reference. Article 16: Private schools or other organizations that run their own people's schools may request the association for subsidies for teaching supplies if they are indeed in financial difficulties and cannot support themselves, but they must be subject to the supervision of the association, or directly use the name established by the association. Article 17: Any matters not covered in this outline may be amended at any time. Article 18: This outline shall be implemented upon resolution by this council.

(Vienna, 7th) The 20th Congress of the International Olympic Committee opened today in the Great Hall of the Academy of Sciences in Vienna. Spring and Autumn

Popularity 208

— Yang Yusheng

People must have "qi" (vital energy/spirit). Conversely, without "qi," one certainly cannot be considered human!

However, most people today are ruined by the lack of "qi"! No wonder, because they are not human at all! And those who have a little "popularity" are not allowed to have "qi." They may have a share in farting, but "breathing" is difficult to approve. So everyone holds their breath, and as a result, in the eyes of Westerners, there are no "people" in China, because most Chinese people have no "qi." Don't believe me, look up!

I believe that spiritual distress is the most difficult to endure. Therefore, I thought of a story about an imported product, to share with those who are generally bloated:

It is said that in Wisconsin, USA, there was a certain sports association with a referee. He was so small and weak that, placed among many strong and robust athletes, he felt the same "hair-raising" sensation as the ailing Republic of China, surrounded by powerful foreign powers with covetous eyes. But he was, after all, a person with "popularity." He was impartial in his work and never flinched because the athletes were unruly. One day, he ruled that an athlete had committed a foul and ordered him to stop the game immediately. The athlete refused to accept the ruling and used all sorts of unbearable language to scold the referee. He endured it and, after consideration, resolutely said to the violent athlete, "I want to duel with you. You have insulted me too much." The athlete heard that the referee wanted to duel with him, suddenly stopped his scolding, examined the referee in surprise, and asked him very strangely, "Really want to duel with me? You..." "Yes, I must duel with you. You have insulted me," the other party replied resolutely. So, amidst the athlete's loud laughter, the duel began! The small, weak referee was beaten until his nose was bruised and his eyes were swollen, his face covered in blood. He was knocked down, got up, got up, and was knocked down again. Ah! In the eyes of Chinese people, wouldn't he be an "idiot"! However, he was, after all, a person with "popularity"! He knew that dueling with the other party was in danger of "losing his life," but he felt that his personality had been bullied too much. Although he knew he was going to die, he still resolutely dueled with the other party... dueled... dueled... until he groaned and couldn't hold on, and he didn't have the strength to get up and fight again, the other party also collapsed to the ground! Afterwards, the sports community in Wisconsin publicly sentenced the athlete to imprisonment and awarded the referee a gold medal for bravery!

This story full of "popularity" is really great! I used to talk about it to people in words or writing. At the same time, I think this referee is really worthy of admiration! We Chinese people don't have this kind of silliness!

Some people say that China is ruined by the lack of such fools. I think the person who said this may be a fool himself!

Drizzle 209

— Fu Yizhi

At the entrance of a certain theater, red and white electric lights formed the large characters of "Qu Bianzi Massage Parlor." More than a dozen yellow-uniformed policemen, with Mauser pistols and similar weapons at their waists, stood on the left and right sides of the theater entrance. (Note: The authorities used armed force to prevent the performance from starting.) The roads on both ends were crowded with wriggling people. I was using my dull eyes, trying my best to shoot forward, but a burst of sharp singing came from behind, full of ups and downs, "Drizzle, falling endlessly, gentle wind, blowing endlessly, gentle wind and light rain, green willows..."

This delicate singing entered my eardrums, and I turned my head involuntarily to explore the origin of the singing. Unexpectedly, it turned out to be a thin, pale-faced old man with disheveled hair and a curly beard, wearing a torn and dirty long gown, walking back and forth while closing his throat and pretending to be emotional.

"Old man! Although you are also spending your remaining life in this bustling market, you are only embellishing the noise. Society no longer has a place for you. Are you singing like this as if you were living in the days of Wu Huai and Ge Tian? Or are you like Qu Lingjun wandering by the riverside, with unspeakable bitterness in your heart, and using this to vent your complaints?" I almost shouted out.

Life is like a sojourn, one should not create one's own troubles. Su Shi said, "If you pour a basin of water on the ground, mustard will float on the water, and ants will float on the mustard, clueless as to where to go. In a moment, the water dries up, and the ants leave. Seeing their kind, they cry, saying, 'I almost didn't see you again!' How can they know that in the blink of an eye, there are roads in all directions?" With this kind of optimism, no matter how poor you are, you will be happy everywhere. When it comes to national affairs, there are already many officials in charge. The Tanggu Truce Agreement has already been signed. From this, the world is at peace, and there is no need for us poor people to worry. However, general pessimists, knowing that depression is useless, insist on making sick groans. I am also one of them. Why? I don't know myself... "Old man! You are truly a transcendent immortal. I envy you. I am following you, I am chasing you, I want you to lead me to the world of bliss!"

The Bee's Sting 210

— Drunken Fool

The art of facial expressions is most emphasized by shop clerks. They have two sets of "cold" and "hot" faces, one for male customers and one for female customers. But among female customers, there are also two types of faces. One is for those who are looked down upon, and the other is for the elderly.

Modern women are important figures in society. If there are no modern women to embellish it, society will be dull and lifeless.

The people in society, bustling and bustling, come and go, all relying on wearing masks. If the masks are removed, it will no longer be society.

Although women have the name of "vases," vases must have considerable qualifications, not everyone can be one. If they don't meet these qualifications, they are like earthenware pots and jars. They can only be used for practical purposes in the family, not for people to appreciate.

The signs of "florists" and "lawyers" in Shanghai will gradually increase every year. This shows that the morbidity of society is not light!

Last year, Shaanxi Province experienced a tragic epidemic disaster. When cholera began to spread, the local authorities, in order to arouse public attention, specially selected a pair of tigers from the zoo, put them in cages, and paraded them through the city and countryside. This kind of action was very effective in terms of public education, but in fact, due to the poor transportation in the northwest and the difficulty in transporting medicines, the people of Shaanxi died in the hundreds of thousands under such poor epidemic prevention conditions!

Small Gardening

The Secret of Flower Seeds 214

— Bingyu

Generally, plant seeds are thought to be hard, solid, and lifeless. However, all seeds contain life, but the duration of seed life varies depending on the storage method. Most seeds last for one or two years, or at most three or four years. Some seeds die within three or four months after harvesting. When seeds are sown and receive the proper temperature and moisture, they will naturally germinate. Therefore, if seeds are stored in a container where they receive the right conditions for germination, the nutrients in the seeds will begin to decompose, just as if they were in the ground. If the storage container is too dry, the seeds will die. In China, the climate during the plum rain season is characterized by increasing humidity and temperature, during which the nutrients in seeds often decompose and germinate. Then, in the hot summer, they easily dry out and die. Therefore, it is important to pay close attention to seed preservation during this period.

Identifying Good and Bad Seeds

In home gardening, we should have the knowledge to distinguish seeds, to know whether a particular seed is viable or dead. This distinction is not easy to make without accurate experience. Here, I will explain the common and easily distinguishable characteristics that one should know. First, look at the color of the seeds. Is it bright and lively? Second, if there is mold on the surface of the seeds, they will not grow well. Third, if the outside is not clear, you can use a small knife to cut open the outer skin and see if the flesh inside has changed color. Generally, it should be white. If it has turned black, it has died due to excessive dryness. Fourth, you can crush the seed with wood or stone. If there is not much moisture or oil, then the seed is also useless.

Seed Dormancy

Various seeds have a dormancy period. For example, some seeds can be sown immediately after harvesting and will grow well. However, some seeds require a certain period before they can germinate. This is the phenomenon of seed dormancy. In general, various plants flower from spring to summer and bear fruit from summer to autumn. Some seeds that fall to the ground can germinate and grow immediately, while others can only germinate in the spring of the following year. If we collect seeds for testing, about 80% to 90% will require a certain period before they can germinate.

Seed Preservation Method

There are many methods for preserving seeds, depending on the type of seed. The most common methods involve using materials that can absorb moisture, such as lime and rice straw ash, sealing them in jars, and placing them in a cool place. For ordinary simple preservation, seeds can be stored in earthenware or porcelain jars, but the mouth of the jar must be sealed with oiled paper to prevent moisture from entering, and then placed in a cool corner of the house. In the past, meticulous people often stored them in boxes made of paulownia wood, because paulownia wood has moisture-proof properties, preventing outside moisture from entering and causing the seeds to decompose.

Seed Germination Rate

When sowing seeds, you must choose the shape of the seeds. Generally, large seeds are fully mature and develop more quickly. Small seeds may be somewhat immature. About 20% to 30% of these seeds cannot germinate. However, the germination rate of seeds varies depending on the type. Morning glories, zinnias, cosmos, and vegetables such as cabbage, radish, and turnip have a germination rate of 80% to 90%. However, the speed of germination often varies depending on the season, humidity, soil, and other factors.

Germination Experiment and Sowing Method

Germination experiments for seeds are inherently very difficult, due to the different properties of the seeds and the differences in climate and humidity. The same seeds often behave differently. Here, I will introduce a common and simple method. First, take 100 seeds (without mustard or soil) and spread them on absorbent paper. Place the paper in a dish, ensuring that the bottom of the dish has adequate moisture. At the same time, cover it with a piece of glass to prevent it from drying out. Place it in a room with a temperature of about 60 degrees Fahrenheit. Some seeds will germinate after four or five days, while others may take two or three weeks or a month. We can then calculate the percentage and determine the germination rate. If sowing in soil, the soil should not be fertile and should not be sown too deep. Only cover it with one or two points of loose soil, just enough to cover the seeds. Cover the top with rice straw. For small seeds, cover the top with newspaper without covering the soil. Spray with water in the morning and evening. Before germination, avoid direct sunlight. However, before sowing, it is best to gently cut the outer skin with a knife and soak it in water for twelve hours. This will make it easier to germinate.
