Securities and Bond Markets Gradually Entering a Peaceful State 220

Yesterday, the Chinese Securities Exchange saw an increasingly peaceful market. Both bulls and bears adopted a wait-and-see approach, and investor sentiment was lax. This is an inevitable stage after a period of volatility. Overall, the trend was weak but firm, with no exciting developments. In the morning, the listed securities initially fell by three to five jiao. Later, starting with the 20 series, various merchants showed a stronger appetite for buying, and there was no shortage of scattered buyers, gradually boosting prices by one or two jiao to around six jiao. Consequently, the situation changed slightly in the second session. The 1920 readjustment loan surged by as much as eight or nine jiao, showing signs of recovery, but this was primarily due to swap and arbitrage activity, resulting in occasional abnormal conditions. Later, the 20-year treasury bonds rose, but supply still exceeded demand, causing them to fall slightly by three or four jiao. In the afternoon, except for the 1920 customs loan, which saw a slight rebound of over three jiao, the remaining securities continued to fall by three or four jiao. However, the salt tax bonds were relatively strong, slightly boosting investor sentiment. The closing prices increased across the board by two or three jiao to around five jiao, indicating a potential recovery. If the salt tax bonds can break through the 50 yuan level again, there could be a further increase of one or two yuan. Overall, the day's market prices resulted in increases ranging from two or three jiao to six or seven jiao, with only the 1918 customs consolidation and disarmament bonds falling by about five fen or two jiao. The Jiangzhe silk industry public bonds issued in 1921, with a total value of 3 million, began trading in the spot market yesterday. Due to the limited amount, there were no futures transactions. The market price was 72.6 yuan. The total transaction volume was 4,449,100 yuan, including 16,000 yuan in spot transactions and 5.205 million for futures, consolidated salt tax, 1.96 million for disarmament, 2.85 million for 19 customs loan readjustment, 3.14 million for 20 customs, and the remainder ranged from tens of thousands to 835,000, 485,000.

Silk, Tea, and Silkworm Cocoon News Combined 224

(Jiahu Cocoon Market Gradually Comes to an End) The cocoon season in Jiaxing and Huzhou is about ten days later than in Hangzhou and Shaoxing. This year's cocoon production is generally only 40-50%. The best cocoons are from Nanxun in Huzhou. The cocoon market is gradually ending. The highest cocoon price for improved varieties is 50 yuan, and the lowest for local varieties is 24-25 yuan.

(Many Haining Residents Spun Their Own Native Silk) Late silkworm development is quite good. Silkworm farmers' costs are not low, but cocoon prices are not high, 20-30 yuan lower than last year. Therefore, they are all taking them home to bake using local methods and are mostly spinning their own native silk. Cocoon shops are collecting only a little over a thousand dan, and some are collecting less than a hundred dan.

(Most of the Shaoyang Cocoon Shops Have Stopped Weighing) Cocoon shops in the surrounding villages have been open for business for ten days. This year's cocoon production is still abundant, and the amount collected by each shop is not small. Most have already stopped weighing. The average cocoon price is 40 yuan. (Jiangning Foreign Variety Cocoons Are of the Highest Quality) Improved varieties account for 80-90%. Cocoon production is better. The baking loss is only 280 jin. The highest price for high-quality cocoons is 45 yuan, and for local varieties, it is 28-29 yuan.

(Sichuan Raw Silk from Factories Continues to Flow Smoothly) The Shanghai warehouse inventory was originally thick, and then through the

European firms' continuous operations, raw silk is

Almost sold out. Iron machine, wood machine rebound and small car factories etc. also have small inventory. Production area inventory is not low. Each silk factory will soon start reeling new cocoons. Old goods are transported from Li to Shanghai. Recently, a total of 273 pieces of Sichuan raw silk have arrived.

Trades included 100 bales of Shanghai white raw silk, 120 bales of Shandong yellow raw silk, 200 bales of white spun silk, and 20 bales of Sichuan raw silk, all at prices that continued to rise by 20 yuan.

Discourse

"National Destiny" and "People's Destiny" 233

— Huan Yi

In this civilized era of the Republic of China, talking about fate is simply out of touch with the times, or at least it is a backward person with a dull mind.

But, in my opinion: Destiny is indeed a truly believable thing. Of course, things must be based on evidence.

A person's so-called wealth, nobility, longevity, and short life are all destined in their fate long ago. Moreover, not only is this true for humans, but also for small ants, static objects like a cup or a table, and large entities like a country. All have their own destiny. If their fate is good and their luck is smooth, no matter how they stumble, they will never encounter bad luck. But, what if the opposite is true? Then it's terrible, no matter what you do, medicine and stone are useless, and you can only suffer until you die. This is a great theory for those who are proficient in the way of fate.

China's "national destiny" can probably not be said to be good! As for "national luck"? That's also terrible. Just open up the history books and take a look. It's really lively, like a red-faced man fighting a white-faced man on a stage, and a white-faced man chasing a black-faced man. It's been like this for thousands of years, and we've simply never had good luck. In 633 years, we had the misfortune of being ruled by foreign races twice. Fortunately, Heaven never abandons a nation. After the bad luck was shed, we ushered in the good luck of the Great Republic of China. But, after all, because the "national destiny" is too bitter, the grand luck has also turned into a weak luck. For 22 years, we have almost lost half of our national life. This is probably called bad luck!

Next, let's talk about our "people's destiny." Of course, the fate of the parents is indescribably bitter, so the fate of the children can only be slightly better. Let's not talk about the past, let's just talk about recent encounters. The poor, suffering people who deserve to suffer, when they bid farewell to Yama and came to the Yang world in large numbers, probably had a Yama ticket attached to them, as if they had signed a contract to "live" and "die" and be "slaves of a fallen country" together. Just look at the drought in Shaanxi and Gansu a few years ago, where millions died of starvation in one batch, and the great flood in central China the year before last, where millions were submerged again. Since the September 18th Incident, the four northeastern provinces have been lost due to the lack of "national luck." The number of people who have been invited to become slaves of a fallen province is over 30 million. Poor little people who deserve to suffer disasters, who are you going to blame for your own bitter fate?

Therefore, whether they are refugees, disaster victims, or slaves of a fallen province, they are all victims of their own misfortune, and it has nothing to do with anyone else. In other words: because their own fate is bitter, they have attracted many disasters, and this has affected the lack of "national luck." It is useless for others to help them. Therefore, expelling refugees and prohibiting refugees from landing are really urgent tasks that various places cannot delay at present. Because thieves already have a poor, sour air, and refugees and disaster victims are all wearing a crying face. They are all full of the air of disaster. If they are infected by them, then it will really be a big problem. Moreover, in a metropolis that is promoting high-class entertainment and lifting the ban on prostitution, wouldn't it be a great disappointment?

It's not worth talking about bitter fate. Let's change the topic and talk about good fate. Here, I am very happy to borrow the weight of our young marshal again. Like begets like, the son of a great marshal is of course a young teacher. Precisely because he is a young marshal, after all, his fate is worlds apart from the fate of refugees, disaster victims, and slaves of a fallen province, and they cannot be compared at all. Although the three northeastern provinces are lost, he is still extraordinary. Not only does he not become a slave of a fallen province, but he can also live freely outside the situation. Although the little people are in an uproar for a while, the letters and telegrams are like snowflakes, and the impeachment documents of the Supervisory Yuan are really like the saying goes, "throwing Beijing bricks as New Year's greetings." But, because his fate is prosperous and he is blessed by lucky stars, even a hair has not been shaken. This is a concrete proof.

Alas! Poor little people, who are you going to blame?

Man and God 234

— Wei

I often have to pass through a short street. In addition to some small shops as usual, there is a dim church, with a gray steeple towering above. On one side of the church, a uniform building houses a primary school. Children gather like ants in the hallways, running, bouncing small balls, fighting, and quarreling.

In the morning, the streetcar carries me from a far distance to the vicinity of the church. I and two other children get off. When I ask them why they came so far, I get a candid answer: it's just because of their faith.

Hypocrites, under the protection of God, simple, loyal, kind, and tolerant subjects, children are suffering because of strict religious education.

I sometimes encounter some elderly and virtuous agents of God's authority - priests. It is really a great pleasure. One evening, I met one again. Because an old beggar woman was squatting by the side of the street begging, the priest was furious and called the police to take her away in a depressed manner. The priest must have been worrying, thinking that God had already condemned her to enough suffering, how dare she commit a crime near the church! The people of your country pretend not to see and talk and laugh as if nothing had happened, or perhaps there are one or two stifled resentments or sighs, very lightly, without hearing a sound.

In this way, the street cannot find a person who does not rely on capital or ability to eat. The priest is diligently working for the face and peace of the street.

Then, one day, I don't know what festival it is, the bright and solemn bells are striking, and extravagant light is emitted in front of the glorious altar. I enter the church for the first time. Everyone is devoutly praying and performing Mass. A ridiculous and serious atmosphere envelops the space. The priest at the main altar uses various gestures to bless people and beg for God's forgiveness. The crowd is hypnotized and numb.

"Lord! Listen! The rich are innocent, the evidence is that the Lord has given them money, so punish the guilty with poverty until death. The poor are guilty people, and may the Lord not bless them, let them live a few more years, and then transcend. Amen!"

Literary Arts

Welcome Generals Ma Zhanshan and Su Bingwen 235

— Shen Min

The masses cheer and warmly welcome, the generals return home to celebrate their remaining lives. Their heroic names and military strategies shake the world, and they will come back and conquer again.

They glorify the nation as heroes, and their names will be passed down in history as admirable. Recalling the battle of the Nenjiang Bridge, they bravely fought the enemy and made great contributions.

Skilled in battle, courageous and bold, they did not hesitate to go through fire and water. It was only because the reinforcements were cut off and the bullets were exhausted that, although defeated, they were still glorious and righteous.

Looking east, the disaster victims are pitiful, and they are suffering from an unprecedented catastrophe. Raising soldiers to defend against foreign enemies and drive out the strong enemies is a responsibility that should be shouldered to recover our territory,

Living Suffering, Loyal Sail 236

For the "Wedding Wine" 237

— Xue

Auntie Li suddenly received a happy greeting, which turned out to be from her nephew, Fei, whom she used to hold in her arms, who was about to get married, and the wedding date was so close. "Hey! Take a look, this invitation." Auntie Li said, pointing to the newly delivered wedding invitation, looking at her husband.

"Oh? Is Fei really getting married?" At this time, he had some disbelief in his expression, as if he was wondering how a child who was not yet of age and whose finances were not yet independent could get married right away. In that moment of his suspicion, she said like this:

"Don't you believe it? They have money. In this realistic society, with money, even getting a beautiful woman is easy, let alone marrying a daughter-in-law?"

Page 18

"Indeed, I can't deny what you said, of course."

"In that case, we, who are called uncle and aunt, should give a good gift."

"What should we give? But our economy is so tight. If we give a lot, how will we be able to do it?"

"It's difficult enough! In Shanghai, the usual etiquette of giving gifts requires at least a pair of glasses (two yuan), let alone the situation is different now. We are close relatives, and we are also 'elders', so we must at least give a hand (five yuan) to make it presentable."

"Alas, under this current social system, this kind of etiquette of giving gifts, which is close to extortion, is always unbreakable. If we reach another new society, for things like marriage, the parties only need to register with the XX organization, and there is no such thing as giving or not giving gifts at all."

"How can you say that? It sounds like you're trying to escape giving a gift, so you're singing such a high-pitched tune, haha!"

"Although you're still smiling at me slightly now, the inner disappointment is still very clearly visible."

"No. The problem is not just giving the gift, there's also a related matter of giving the gift that needs to be discussed urgently. Guess what!"

"What? I don't know."

"It's the problem of clothes. The weather is getting warmer day by day. The 'Indian silk' cheongsam I made last year is old and small again. How can I wear it to receive the meeting gift from my nephew's new wife?"

"······" He remained silent, as if it was none of his business.

"If you're not going to speak up, we have to think of a solution. Our reputation is at stake."

"Isn't Sister Cheng Er has a new dress that she just put on? Her figure is about the same as yours. You might as well borrow it. After all, you know each other very well."

"Oh! That's so cheap? Miss Cheng Er's clothes have always been more precious than a dragon robe and phoenix coronet. Please come up with another brilliant plan!"

"Then we'll have to quickly publish a notice to sever our relationship as nephew and uncle, otherwise, it would really be 'dying for face and living in suffering'...'"

Female Fortune Teller 238

— Ling Yi

Yesterday, around four or five in the afternoon, I had just finished classes at school and returned home. As I was about to step through the main gate, I suddenly heard a commotion from next door, with sounds of "still barren," "afraid of being childless," "a clash in the palace of fate," and other superstitious ramblings. I thought, "I wonder what new oddity has emerged to provide material for my poor struggling writer to submit."

Driven by curiosity, and also to understand the matter thoroughly, I immediately ran to the home of Mother Ma next door.

Oh, if I hadn't looked, I might have been fine, but one look left me dumbfounded. The room was packed with people—men, women, old, young, old ladies, young mistresses—but mostly old ladies and young mistresses. In the center of the room sat a Yangzhou woman, about forty or fifty years old, holding a box in her hands. Inside the box were paper scrolls, various almanacs, and a thousand mud paper copies, and a leather "spiritual officer" in a three-in-one form. Sitting opposite her was a young mistress of about twenty-seven or twenty-eight years old. I only heard the female fortune teller from Yangzhou say to the young mistress, "Young mistress, don't worry or fret. According to your age and birth month, your palace of fate is clashing with the 'child-harming star.' That's why you haven't conceived in the seven or eight years since you've been married. If you want to have sons and daughters, you must resolve this 'earth-defeating star,' then there is hope. Otherwise, you may never conceive..." The young mistress immediately asked, "Then how can the 'harming star' be resolved?" The female fortune teller replied, "There's no other way. You must consult the spiritual officer, only then will we know."

So, the fortune teller took the three-in-one spiritual officer out of the box. I just saw her mutter for a while into its ear, then she turned to the young mistress and said, ""

Just now the spiritual officer said that your harming star can be resolved, but it's too severe and will cost at least eight yuan in tinfoil fees, plus my handling fee of two yuan, totaling ten yuan. It cannot be done without it." "That's a bit too expensive. I can't scrape together ten yuan right now. Can you lower the price..." said the young mistress. The female fortune teller said, "This is what the spiritual officer requires. How can the price be lowered? My handling fee of two yuan is already the bare minimum. It can't be reduced any further. If you're not sincere, the spiritual officer will get angry, and that's not a joke."

The female fortune teller said solemnly, "Alright, then, let's do it this way," said the young mistress. So, the female fortune teller took the spiritual officer and circled it around the young mistress's body, up and down, front and back, thousands of times, then said, "Your harming star has been resolved. Here are eight pills, you two should each take four of them on [day and month omitted], that night, you're guaranteed to conceive a son. If you give birth to a boy, I'll come to collect the celebration money and have a cup of celebratory wine. Haha?" The female fortune teller, displaying her supernatural powers, said very triumphantly.

The young mistress then took ten silver dollars and handed them to the female fortune teller. The female fortune teller, beaming, thanked her and left.

I watched closely from the side and couldn't help but sigh.

Two hours, ten silver dollars. Even a university professor doesn't make that much. What about small teachers like us?

Female Worker, Jiao Di 239

— Ren Ying

Breaking the silence of the air, a loud whistle sounded; the gates of the XX First Factory spewed out a group of male and female workers completely exhausted and sinking into excessive fatigue. Jiao Di was one of the female workers, an unfortunate girl who had fled from a declining rural village. Introduced by a fellow villager, Li Xiaobao, she had been wearing away her remaining youth in the clatter of machinery for three months!

At this moment, she was carrying a green enamel lunch box, exiting the factory gate; walking alone on the cement sidewalk along the side of the road, heading towards the nearby slum.

After a stretch of road, she turned into an alley. The neighbors living here were all from the working masses laboring in the factory. Jiao Di entered through the back door of the third house. It was early summer, and although the sun had already sunk below the horizon, the sky was not yet covered by a grey twilight. The streetlights on the road shone lonely on the oiled asphalt.

Jiao Di's mother, a middle-aged woman, similarly a bitter soul pushed out of the countryside, had already prepared dinner for her laboring daughter.

It was the middle of the night, just when the excitement of the dance hall was waning and the city was opening for the night. But in a dead and silent slum, everything was as quiet as death. Jiao Di lay on the wooden bed, her two dark eyes constantly gazing at the ceiling.

Mr. Lin, the supervisor at the factory, who was always known for being strict and impartial, why was he so humble towards her today? His usual sternness was gone, and he even promised her the beautiful dream she had longed for. Suddenly, Jiao Di remembered a story told by her little sisters.

Half a year ago, there was a Wuxi female worker named Zhang Guifang who was favored by Supervisor Lin. One stormy night, in the Dongfang Hotel, he achieved his ultimate goal. The next day, her husband found out and angrily went to the factory to cause trouble but was stopped. When the wife, humiliated and resentful, went to work, she was dismissed. Zhang Guifang committed suicide in anger, and her husband was plotting revenge.

Jiao Di thought of this and felt a darkness descend, as if her future was buried in darkness. The sky, illuminated by the city's neon lights, condensed into red clouds, while Jiao Di in the slum stared blankly at the solitary lamp.

Store Clerk Correspondence

Three Legal Questions 241

Editor:

Because you are our kind guiding light, I have several questions to ask you. Please don't refuse and give me clear instructions!

(1) Our ancestral temple is jointly owned by factions A, B, and C. Faction A is further divided into sub-factions Zi, Chou, and Yin. The temple was burned down by bandits due to troop deployment the year before last. Now, each faction wants to rebuild, but some in the minority faction under A oppose the reconstruction. The matter has become an official case. I don't know if the minority faction can legally oppose it.

(2) Our clan is divided into five branches: Heaven, Earth, Ruler, Parent, and Teacher. The Heaven, Earth, and Ruler branches share the same family genealogy, while the Parent and Teacher branches have their own. Unexpectedly, the Ruler branch has died out and has no relatives, so no one is inheriting it. Now, there is someone older than the deceased who is going to inherit (that is, the stepfather is over fifty years old, while the stepson is over sixty years old, the seniority is appropriate). What do you think the legal outcome of this matter would be if it became a lawsuit?

(3) A friend of mine is a street vendor in Shanghai. Last year, through an introduction, he became involved with a widow, intending to marry her and continue his lineage. Until this year, he learned that the woman had taken cold medicine and could not have children. Since this is contrary to the purpose of continuing the lineage, he wants to separate. However, the woman refuses and is holding the matchmaker responsible. Although the man and woman have had a relationship, it is only cohabitation and there is no formal marriage or contract. Separation is unavoidable. Is there any legal responsibility? I am afraid that if it cannot be resolved, it will have to be taken to court!

I would be grateful if you could give your kind guidance on the above three questions. With best wishes,

Sincerely, Qiming

X X X X

Correspondence address: 200 Chuanjiang Road, Pudong

Editor's Note: The nature of ancestral temples can promote the power of national solidarity. The late Premier Sun Yat-sen also gave considerable encouragement in his Three Principles of the People. However, although this kind of thing is good, it can only be regarded as an adornment for the propertied class and cannot be considered an indispensable organization. So, it is a good thing that your family temple was destroyed and you want to rebuild it. However, all expenses should be collected by those who agree. Legally, the minority who oppose it cannot be forced to pay.

According to current laws, a person's estate, unless the deceased made a will during their lifetime designating an heir, should be determined in the following order: (1) direct descendants, (2) direct ascendants, (3) spouse, (4) siblings; relatives beyond the fifth degree are not included. According to the letter, the Ruler branch has become estranged from the other branches. If the deceased did not have a will, the estate should be considered "unclaimed property" and the authorities should be asked to dispose of it according to law. Distant relatives may not interfere. When Mr. X met the woman, he probably expressed his desire to marry her. Therefore, it is best to resolve this matter through negotiation. Otherwise, she can accuse Mr. X of "using fraudulent means to make a person submit to fornication."

Regulations for Soliciting Contemporary Calligraphy and Painting Manuscripts 242

1. This publication specially opens a column to promote national culture and enhance readers' appreciation, publishing masterpieces of calligraphy and painting by famous contemporary writers.

2. Contemporary famous writers and artists who wish to announce their works should send photographs to this publication. It would be especially welcome if they could briefly describe the writer's short biography and style.

3. For contemporary works such as wall hangings, screen strips, etc., photographs must be taken. For other fan surfaces, ruler pages, vertical strips, etc., original works or photos are acceptable.

4. Contemporary works with excellent composition, creation, and elegant brushwork are preferred; otherwise, they will not be included. However, works that are too meticulous or too light and distant may not be published due to the blurring of the printing plate.

5. There is no remuneration for contemporary calligraphy and painting works.

6. If you want to return the photos or original works, please include registered postage.

Novel

The Life of the Five Sisters (28th installment) 243

— Ling He

Although Wu Gui was a worldly-wise person, he was truly puzzled to see the Fifth Mistress and the Second Mistress being so intimate, completely like biological sisters. How many concubines are there who can't help but be jealous, even to the point of domestic unrest and chaos, but these two mistresses were able to show sincerity and respect; the last time the Fifth Mistress bothered the Second Mistress for a visit, today the Fifth Mistress returned the favor.

This banquet was truly lavish. Even Zhang Wenbin, who was secretly invited by Su Lao, was included. There were only three people, but so much food was served that they only ate a bite or two of each dish before instructing the maids to take it away. However, tonight they consumed two full bottles of wine. Since it was sweet, the Second Mistress couldn't resist the Fifth Mistress's encouragement and drank a few more cups. But she always thought that this wine must be mixed with whiskey, otherwise how could it be so easy to get drunk? Indeed, the Second Mistress felt a little tipsy.

The Fifth Mistress also knew a little about Zhang Shao's character from the servants' gossip, but now, after his own very reasonable explanation, she couldn't help but suspect that Minister Su was getting more confused as he got older. Could it be that two young men and women together must have immoral behavior? This was an overstatement.

Moreover, Zhang Wenbin's character was very pleasing to the Second Mistress. How could such an intelligent and handsome young man be willing to do such scandalous things? Because she trusted him too much, she couldn't help but look at him a few more times. She saw his delicate eyes shining with watery, intoxicating light, his cheeks flushed, and she couldn't help but admire him secretly.

"Truly, a beauty of China!"

However, in Zhang Wenbin's eyes, the Second Mistress also had a unique charm. Although she was a bit older, she had a foreign flair. Thinking of this, Zhang Shao felt a tingling sensation that he couldn't explain. If this woman were Miss Liu, then he would be too happy.

Afterward, everyone felt that they couldn't eat anymore, so the Fifth Mistress personally left her seat and started a Western dance record, allowing Zhang Shao to dance with the Second Mistress, while she lay on the sofa smoking. Soon, she simply left the room, closed the door, and went to the bathroom. Then, Zhang Shao naturally became bolder, dancing, dancing, hugging tightly while dancing. The beating of his heart was so rapid that he could barely breathe.

It was almost ten o'clock, and the Fifth Mistress urged Zhang Shao to send the Second Mistress back. However, the Fifth Mistress still felt strangely uncomfortable, watching the Second Mistress happily take Zhang Wenbin's arm and walk out the door. Fortunately, Minister Su soon returned from visiting the home of a government official. He would inevitably pester her for another night. Otherwise, how would she survive this annoying long night?

President Roosevelt's Good Neighbor Policy 244

— Zhu Xian

Foreign Stars Have Regained Their Sense That America Is Livable

The Department of Labor Has Stopped Thoroughly Investigating the Nationality of Film Stars

What is the current status of the thorough investigation of the nationality of film stars that was rumored in Hollywood, America, not long ago? This question was rife with rumors a few months ago, and it caused panic among many foreign stars, technicians, and artists. Several people, fearing a loss of face, took the opportunity to leave the United States and return to their country in advance, and many were reluctant to leave and quietly waited for the punishment of "deportation." Now, it seems that no one is mentioning this issue anymore.

The thorough investigation of the nationality of Hollywood film stars initially occurred in the U.S. Department of Labor, which was also one of the last public cases of the Hoover administration. It should be noted that the U.S. Department of Labor has great power, and all matters related to foreigners entering the country and immigration are within its jurisdiction. Although its original purpose was to protect domestic laborers from the intrusion of foreign laborers, in reality, it was a manifestation of the anti-foreign movement. Initially, various immigration regulations were specifically aimed at Asians, so it was very difficult for Chinese workers to enter the United States, and they were often imprisoned for some violations of regulations and waited to be sent back to China on the original ship. Now, the immigration regulations have become stricter, and people from European countries are also subject to restrictions, and it is not limited to workers, but involves people in the film industry. It is said that in principle, whether they are actors, technicians, or workers in the film industry, or ordinary laborers, they are the same - one more foreigner eating means one less local person eating. Therefore, the Department of Labor wanted to expel all foreign stars, technicians, etc., but forgot their great contributions to helping and creating the American film industry's hegemony!

Now it's good. Since President Roosevelt took office, Ms. Francis Perkins has been appointed as the Minister of Labor. Mr. Garsen, the Deputy Director who was most active in expelling foreign actors, has been transferred to another position and replaced by a more moderate person. After taking office, Ms. Francis Perkins immediately informed the Hollywood film industry that the thorough investigation that had been vigorously implemented had been stopped. She also said that the country is now in a time of many troubles, and they cannot attend to such small matters, and so on.

In President Roosevelt's inaugural address, we can find the words "good neighbor." Since he uses "good neighbor" as his motto, of course, it is not appropriate for him to scold the neighbor's children in Hollywood and send them back to their neighbors by pulling their ears. Moreover, if the United States does this, it is tantamount to suicide. Currently, European countries such as England and Germany are still making every effort to recruit outstanding American film talents. People such as gold-throated Ginny MacDonald, dance queen Pipita Niel, and Constance Cummings, Anda Lewis, etc., have already been absorbed by Europe. If the United States further intends to reject national talents, wouldn't it be seeking its own decline and promoting its own decline?

Film Review

Review of "The Big Drive" 245

— Ling He

Big Drive

On-site photography in the European War

Edited from newsreels

Editing fragmented newsreels into an entire film has been recognized as a new film-making method in the Soviet Union, but it is a difficult task, especially in terms of Montage.

Not long ago, China had various films of volunteer army operations, such as "The Bloody History of the Northeast Volunteer Army," etc. Of course, those works would not satisfy us very much in terms of photography and editing, but they are worthy of our attention in the sense of encouraging revolutionary national wars.

Then, how is "The Big Drive," which premiered at the Carlton yesterday? It is also a war newsreel, plus some model "fantasy photography" and after-the-fact performances of hand-to-hand combat. Because in battlefield photography, Camera men must avoid shell fire, so direct conflict scenes are difficult to capture. In this film, what we can see are troops leaving, inspections by senior officers and even the king. Cannons, tanks, submarines, torpedoes, airplanes, bombs, corpses, crosses in cemeteries.

Indeed, the cruel impression of World War I will never be forgotten in our memory. How many innocent people were driven to the battlefield, although they did not need the war, but in the narrow sense of patriotism, they were encouraged to leave their families and children to kill and even be killed. They bleed, they die, they lie stiff in the trenches, they are buried in mass graves. But the death of every officer is given a soldier's salute, a band's music, a coffin covered with a national flag and a wreath. Of course, this means that those who wear gold-rimmed military hats in life will naturally be majestic and glorious in death. These are most clearly shown in the picture.

As mentioned above, there are many fake scenes in this film, but the editing is still clear, so to understand the true face of this massacre, this silent film with verbal explanation, "The Big Drive," can also be used as reference material.

Hollywood Engages in Cost-Cutting to Avoid Congressional Intervention 246

— Fu Lun

The impact of the global economic collapse has affected the United States, especially Hollywood, the world's film capital. In the past, the U.S. government has adopted a policy of non-interference in Hollywood. Now the attitude has suddenly changed, and Congress is preparing to thoroughly investigate the situation of the Hollywood film industry. The investigation includes the production costs of films, the salaries of film stars, the methods of film sales, etc. The high salaries of film stars are known to everyone in the world, but now the company authorities also know the economic difficulties and are thinking about engaging in austerity. In the future, when renewing contracts, the highest salary will probably not exceed two thousand U.S. dollars per week. This is only one-fifth of the peak era and only one-third of the existing contract. In this way, on the one hand, costs can be saved, and on the other hand, congressional intervention can be avoided. It can be said that it is a well-prepared plan that achieves two goals with one move.

Review of "Going to Die on the Battlefield" and "Street Singer" 247

— Yannan

(Preface) In all war films and martial arts films, the style is mostly monotonous, but this "Going to Die on the Battlefield" (Private Tones) is unique.

(Synopsis) An American coward is forced to enlist. He disagrees with the adjutant but is attracted to the adjutant's wife, leading to intense animosity. Once, he and the adjutant go on a reconnaissance mission and are captured by the Germans. They eventually escape, but because of the poison gas filling the battlefield, they only find one gas mask. He intends to give it to the adjutant, risking his own escape and ultimately dying from the poison.

(Script) In terms of ethics, this film can be considered to have fulfilled its duty, using motherly love as its core from beginning to end. Until death, the gold coin sent by his mother remains in his hand, which is indeed very touching. However, during the performance, because it leaned too much towards humor and jokes, the script became contradictory. The personality of the secondary character, the adjutant, is not explained at all. And is it really possible for a coward to later "Going to Die on the Battlefield" for a friend?

It's a real question. The depiction of military life and the time after being captured is also exaggerated, making it hard to believe that the American army was so undisciplined and the German army so incompetent? This film is compact from beginning to end, but it is all unreasonable. (Purpose) During the performance, the actions and personalities of every type of person in society are vividly conveyed, adding a lot of power to the script. For example, the depiction of a personal secretary [so-called "flower vase"]'s shamelessness, soldiers [so-called "hillbillies"]' rudeness, etc., can all leave a deep impression.

(Director) Throughout the play, the script has already created many mistakes, and of course it is difficult to correct them on set. However, the director is still worthy of our admiration. Every small segment shows the director's cleverness in interweaving, and nothing is lightly let go. All the strengths in the script are developed and expanded one by one. At the end, although the protagonist dies, the script doesn't seem finished, but it stops abruptly, leaving a lingering aftertaste. However, it is a pity that too much attention was paid to the humorous aspects, and the "quantity" was increased along with the "quality." The short plot actually runs for eighty minutes, which is a bit long.

(Technique) The division of scenes is noteworthy. Many double exposures and collages of small shots are quite captivating. Second is the set design. The scene of artillery fire on the battlefield is very clear. The large sections of military music are also extremely tragic, inspiring the cowardly to stand up. The atmosphere is quite tense. Although there is a lot of dialogue, there is no shortage of humorous sentences. Often one side provokes bursts of laughter. However, the inclusion of many military slang terms and extremely offensive vulgar language is not commendable. Although there are many brilliant aspects of the lighting and photography, I think if the film was not old, then it must have been too careless when developing and printing. There are stripes that look like scratches almost everywhere, which is a real demerit. (Performance) Lee Tracy still has that awkward face and is very good at playing a soldier. There are some similarities (like Pascaud in "Gentlemen of the Army") and there are also many extremely deep inner facial expressions, which is a big improvement compared to previous films. His speech is eloquent, his movements are stiff, and he provides a lot of laughs. The rest of the actors are not bad. It can be said to be serious and humorous at the same time.

(Street Singer) A song film replaces the news, and it's all singing. We know that this is the famous song谱阿斯特屈山's golden voice, which is currently the most popular radio broadcast in the United States. You can hear it clearly here. There is no plot, but for the sake of this beautiful music and jazz songs, which are the most popular in the trend, it is introduced in passing. The description of women as temptations also has some lingering flavor.

(Aside) Two good films are still worth seeing, but the magnificent and solemn translated title "Going to Die on the Battlefield" is inappropriate.

Chaplin's Literary Enthusiasm 248

— Luofen

Charlie Chaplin's literary enthusiasm has recently flourished. He hides alone in his home on the top of Beverly Hills, discarding his treasured pair of worn-out leather shoes, cane, and narrow-brimmed black hat, and grasps a pen all day long, doing that brain-racking work. For months, Chaplin has not left his house. Many people thought he was enjoying himself somewhere, but little did they know that he was diligently working with pen and ink, doing the most arduous work!

Chaplin has been writing for several months, and now the manuscript is complete. The book is called "A Comedian Sees the World," and Chaplin has now taken it to New York for publication. Chaplin's writing is highly praised by readers in Europe and America. He is good at using sharp eyes and flexible penmanship to carefully highlight the essence of life, the hypocrisy of the world, and the contradictions of society. In particular, his works depicting the theatrical world, which are scattered in various magazines and newspapers, are even more popular with readers. Therefore, this "A Comedian Sees the World" will surely be a sensation after its publication.

Film Novel: Girls in Uniform (4) 250

— Xin Fu

Produced by German Film Company, starring an all-female cast

A line of dawn, radiating from the east! The dark earth is gradually becoming bright. Everything on the earth seems to be welcoming with a smile: "Light! Light! Come quickly!" Then, a series of wake-up bells broke the sweet dreams of the girls. One by one, they left their lovely beds, took their towels, and headed towards the bathroom. Inside the bathroom, there were rows of wooden cage-like bathing rooms on both sides, with a corridor in the middle. While bathing, many little girls would stretch out their toes to admire the beauty of their curves; some would take out a mirror to look at themselves with infatuation; some would stand in the corridor, giggling and joking. But Manuela, she was leaning against the wall in the bathing room, staring straight at the ceiling above, savoring the taste of last night's kiss.

Around a long table in the office, the principal and several teachers were sitting together, discussing teaching policies. Miss von Bernhard stepped forward and said seriously: "In my opinion, the teachers' room should be a good companion for the students and should not adopt oppressive measures." The principal retorted with an expression of dissatisfaction: "Then how can you maintain your dignity? In such a public group, favoritism can make them suffer from depression. Obeying discipline is the only unchangeable school motto." Those teachers who followed the trend of flattery all agreed repeatedly. Frustrated, Miss von Bernhard argued strongly with them: "But my method has already achieved great success in the exams." Everyone unexpectedly revealed mocking expressions and said: "That's too funny!" Seeing this situation, Miss von Bernhard had no choice but to sigh and remain silent.

This day happened to be Bible class, which was taught by Miss von Bernhard. Miss von Bernhard walked onto the podium and began to question the students' homework. As soon as Manuela saw Miss von Bernhard, she seemed lost. While Miss von Bernhard was questioning other students, she stared infatuatedly at Miss von Bernhard without blinking. When Miss von Bernhard asked about her course, she stammered and could not answer. After Miss von Bernhard finished questioning others, she ran to her side and said to her very gently: "You haven't memorized your homework. I hope you won't do this again next time." Manuela blushed with shame and could not say a word. (To be continued)
